Recent Situation in Suiyuan Discussed by Man Tai

(Taiyuan) Man Tai arrived in Taiyuan from Suiyuan on the 12th and met with Yan [Xishan] to report on the organization of the Mongol Army Border Defense Headquarters, the situation in Suiyuan and the border defense, and to discuss military pay. According to Man, there are currently 5,000 cavalrymen stationed at various checkpoints, the local area is quite peaceful, and there are no Communist elements. However, the social economy is bankrupt and the people's livelihood is worrying. (13th Special Dispatch)

Zhang Zongchang's Coffin Moved to Guanghua Temple

(Beiping) Zhang Zongchang's coffin was moved from the railway station to Guanghua Temple this morning. The various ceremonial guards were not very grand. Among the important figures, only Wan Fulin personally attended and held the ropes. The actor Li Wanchun wore mourning clothes and paid his respects. After the coffin arrived at the temple, Zhang's mother held the coffin and wept bitterly, and his wives and concubines shed tears and looked worried. (13th Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Shen Honglie left for Ji'nan at 10 p.m. on the 13th, and then went to Ping to pay respects to Zhang Zongchang. Peng Dabing and Ge Guangting accompanied him. (13th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee telegraphed the Provincial Party Headquarters today, stating that the Zheng Jicheng case has been approved by the Standing Committee and forwarded to the Executive Yuan, ordering the Ministry of Judicial Administration to handle it according to law. The Provincial Government will send Zheng to the court as soon as it receives the Ministry's notification. (13th Special Dispatch)

Shandong Education Department Plans to Purchase Antiquities

(Jinan) The Ministry of Interior consulted the Provincial Government about the purchase of Chen's antiquities in Weixian County, the current situation of the Mao Gong Ding and the Wanyin Lou, and requested appropriate handling. The Provincial Government ordered the Education Department to investigate. The Education Department decided to convene the Shandong Library Committee to find ways to purchase the Mao Gong Ding, the Wanyin Lou, and the Haiyuan Pavilion collection. (13th Special Dispatch)

Seven More Communists Arrested in Qingzhou

(Jinan) Seven more Communists were arrested in Qingzhou, including the false county committee secretary Duan Wenmin and his mistress. (13th Special Dispatch)

Liu Wenxuan Case Transferred to Headquarters for Trial

(Hankou) It is said that Liu Wenxuan was transferred to the headquarters for trial on the 13th. The criminal part will still be judged by the Wuchang Court according to law. The court plans to announce the facts of the case and the process of acceptance to the whole country to show impartiality. (13th Special Dispatch)

Shantou Student Union Prepares for National Crisis Memorial

(Shantou) The Shantou Student Resistance Conference decided to convene all students in the city to commemorate the September 18th Incident with a grand parade, designated Zhongyuan as the meeting place, and drafted declarations and slogans. (13th Special Dispatch)

Shantou Business Tax Extended Again

(Shantou) The Shantou business tax has been extended again to the 22nd. Strict enforcement will be carried out during the period. Chen Daonan took office as chairman of the Chamber of Commerce. (13th Special Dispatch)

Important Foreign Telegrams: Unprecedented Strange Drama in the German Parliament

Speaker Refuses to Recognize Dissolution Order, Then Softens

Papen Relies on Presidential Support to Exert Authority

Reuters, Berlin, 12th. An unprecedented strange drama occurred in the German Parliament today. Speaker Göring refused to recognize the dissolution order as valid and still convened the parliament to meet tomorrow. His reason was that the government had already failed and therefore could not dissolve the parliament. It is generally believed that the creation of this situation will lead to very serious consequences. Speaker Göring then suddenly changed his mind and decided to cancel his previous resolution. If Göring still adhered to the decision to continue opening the parliament, the government would inevitably prevent it from meeting and, if necessary, resort to force. Therefore, before Göring canceled his previous resolution, people were very worried that the government and the National Socialist Party would have a major conflict. All citizens who advocate peace hope that the National Socialist Party will not go to extremes. The reason why Göring canceled his previous resolution was because he received a letter from Prime Minister Papen, stating that Göring's actions of not allowing the Prime Minister to debate in the parliament and Göring's handling of the Communist Party's no-confidence motion were all illegal acts. The government then announced that after the parliament was dissolved, only the Foreign Affairs Committee could continue to operate as usual. The government will observe the development of the situation tomorrow and then submit a report to President Hindenburg on the date of the next election. Göring told people that he could not accept Papen's accusation that the parliament had adopted illegal procedures. Prime Minister Papen gave a broadcast speech in the evening, addressing the whole country, defending the government's position, emphasizing the necessity of national unity, and requesting that, especially during international disarmament discussions, the whole country must be united. How can we bear it if we are regarded as a second-class country without military protection? The cabinet will decide in a few days how to proceed with this important issue.

Reuters, Berlin, 13th. Although the government has been opposed by the parliament, it is determined to stay in office. Prime Minister Papen now enjoys the full trust of President Hindenburg, as can be seen from the President's signing of the parliament dissolution order in Neudeck and allowing Papen to act as he sees fit. Germans are now debating whether the action of completing a no-confidence vote before announcing the dissolution is justified. The National Socialist Party said that Speaker Göring's actions were justified, while the Center Party said that dissolving the parliament is very harmful to Germany and should be avoided. The National People's Party supports the Prime Minister and asks the whole country to do its best to assist President Hindenburg. The Social Democratic Party now accepts the dissolution order, but the Communist Party asks Speaker Göring to convene the parliament on [blank] day, fearing that Göring will not agree to their request. It is expected that if national security can be maintained, the general election can be held in early November. The government is currently insisting on its demand for military equality. All eyes are on Great Britain, and it is expected that Britain's attitude can open a path to compromise.

National News Agency, Berlin, 12th. Yesterday's dissolution of the parliament was like a bolt from the blue. The general public, including even experienced political observers, were shocked. The news of the dissolution of the parliament and Speaker Göring's refusal to accept President Hindenburg's dissolution order immediately spread throughout the country, causing public unrest. In addition, rumors spread that if the parliament insisted on opposing the government, the government planned to declare martial law. Therefore, the public was even more alarmed. Before long, the Catholic Center Party decided not to add fuel to the fire, and advised Speaker Göring not to go to extremes. The government also announced that it had no intention of implementing extreme plans to defend the country, and then the public's heart gradually stabilized. It is expected that this dispute will be submitted to the National Court, and the parliament only said that the Supervisory Committee will convene a meeting when necessary. The dissolution of the parliament was expected long ago, but it was never expected to happen so quickly and in such a strange way. [Blank] The German parliament has never had a leader of the government refuse to address the chamber. Even other parliaments in the world do not have this kind of [blank] action. [Blank] Currently, people in the political circles generally say that Speaker Göring's refusal to allow the Prime Minister to [blank] speak is a violation of the constitution. Prime Minister Papen also stated in his broadcast [blank] speech that a few days ago, the parliament listened to the speech of Ms. Xiteqing, a Communist Party member and a member of the Third International. The National Socialist Party claims to be the sole representative of the true spirit of the nation, but now one of its main members is preventing the leader of the government from speaking to the members of parliament. Isn't that something to be cautious about? According to various sources close to the government, rumors outside that there will be changes in the cabinet in the near future, and that Defense Minister Schleicher will replace Prime Minister Papen, are absolutely unfounded. In fact, cabinet colleagues and the cabinet and President Hindenburg are now in complete harmony.

National News Agency, Berlin, 13th. The German political situation has been extremely chaotic since the sudden dissolution of the parliament. Today, the Social Democratic Party proposed that at least part of the government's economic plan be submitted to a national referendum, which made the situation even more confusing. The Social Democratic Party in the parliament this morning has asked the Ministry of Interior to draw up a bill to abolish the clauses in the emergency order that change unemployment relief, old-age pensions, disability benefits, etc., and submit it to a national referendum. However, political circles believe that this move may not obtain the legally required number of affirmative votes. This request by the Social Democratic Party is only a step in the next election campaign.

Papen Broadcasts Speech on Major Policies

National News Agency, Berlin, 12th. Prime Minister Papen originally intended to give a speech on his major policies in the parliament this morning, but was prevented from doing so. Tonight, he broadcast this speech to the whole country via radio. He first talked about Germany's demand for military equality, saying that what was decided in Geneva was not disarmament. Germany will no longer attend the disarmament conference until the equality issue is satisfactorily resolved. Fortunately, Germany's position is not isolated and helpless. The Italian government leader has publicly expressed his willingness to support it. The French reply is currently being carefully considered by the cabinet, and its decision will be based on the country's honor and life. The Prime Minister then mentioned the economic reform plan that has been properly decided domestically, saying that the cabinet is determined to fight to solve the disaster of unemployment, and the situation in all aspects has shown a turning point. At the beginning of the cabinet's administration, there were only 50,000 volunteers, but now it has increased to 200,000. He is now responsible for issuing a very solemn warning, that is, the cabinet's plan, the safety of the country's future, depends on this, so we must implement it with all our strength. The Prime Minister then earnestly said that if the cabinet's plan fails, private enterprises will perish together. Then he attacked the National Socialist Party, saying that the party opposes the government's plan, which contains many ideals, simply because the government is not composed of party members of the party. The Prime Minister warned the members of the National Socialist Party that they should not take class hatred as a trend and fight elections, and should not use Marxist weapons, because if they use these weapons, they will inevitably be ordered by the Marxists. Finally, he said that since the parliament refused to listen to his speech, he especially petitioned the whole country. In the evening, Interior Minister Geer met with representatives of the press to explain the constitutional position to them, saying that the dissolution of the parliament was justified. The cabinet does not want to ignore the guarantees in the constitution in the upcoming election battle, but only allows this battle to proceed in the usual way, and national security must be taken care of first.

French Government Publishes

Full Text of Reply to Germany

Refuses Demand for Military Equality

National News Agency, Paris, 12th. The French government today published the full text of its reply to Germany, the main idea of which is that the principle adopted by France is that it should not move forward to the principle of military rearmament, but should proceed in the direction of restrained general reduction of armaments. The French government is willing to do its best to reduce the burden on the people, and especially hopes to see a universal peace organization, so that security is guaranteed, so that disarmament can go further. Germany should certainly plan its national security, but it must seek international restraint of armaments, promote arbitration, and guarantee the effective implementation of international sanctions from all countries to obtain security. In addition, the reply also refused to discuss the issue of military equality only between the two parties, saying that Germany cannot rearm without the consent of all signatories to the Treaty of Versailles. In any case, there is nothing that can be done except through the League of Nations. Finally, it reiterated that France is willing to cooperate with Germany to find a formula to make war impossible.

Gandhi Vows to Fast

Resist the New Electoral System

Reuters, Simla, 13th. Because the British government has decided to stipulate separate electoral districts for "lower classes" and Muslims, Sikhs, Indian Christians, Anglo-Indians, and Europeans, Gandhi has decided to start a fast from September 20th, vowing to die without change to show his opposition to the British government's determination. The so-called "lower classes" refers to the Indian Hindus. Gandhi's intention is that the British government's decision cannot save the degeneration of the Indian Hindus. Gandhi's intention to fast was stated in his letters to Prime Minister MacDonald and Indian Minister Hall, but MacDonald said in his reply that the British side expressed [blank] about Gandhi's fasting, but in any case, the British government's decision will be maintained, because the British government's decision is to protect the "lower classes". In his letter to MacDonald, Gandhi said, "I will vow to die fasting, and use my life to oppose the British government's decision. I will no longer eat, only drink water mixed with salt and soda, or only drink clean water." Gandhi also said that his fast will begin on September 20th. If the British government agrees to cancel the new electoral system, he will stop fasting immediately. MacDonald, in his reply, asked Gandhi to reconsider his decision, because there may be misunderstandings in the meantime. Gandhi replied to the Prime Minister in a letter on September 9th, saying that he could not change his decision. Gandhi was arrested on January 4th this year for presiding over the passive resistance movement. He may be released on September 20th, so Gandhi decided to start fasting from that day. It is heard that after Gandhi starts fasting, he will move to the Sabarmati Sanatorium on the outskirts of Ahmedabad. The Indian government has now prepared everything to prevent unexpected changes, and it is expected that Gandhi's fasting can be extended for up to a month without endangering his life. What kind of reaction Gandhi's expression will have can be clear today. It is expected that the opposition National Party will propose a recess of the Legislative Council to facilitate the discussion of the new situation. When Sir Reading was the Governor-General of India, Gandhi once fasted, and as a result, a joint conference of various parties was convened. Therefore, it is expected that this time Gandhi's fasting may still lead to the same result to save Gandhi's life. Gandhi's last fasting lasted for twenty-one days.

Japan's Redification Advances Fiercely, Propaganda Against War to Soldiers

Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun said that recently, extreme leftists have been cultivating extreme left red cells in ordnance factories, and they have been very active. Although they have been repeatedly investigated and temporarily restrained, unexpectedly, the Fangbashi military police detachment recently detected the group organization of the "League of Militant Atheists" in the Huogong factory of the Army Ordnance Factory in Wangzi Town, outside the city. Among the members, newspapers such as "Red Flag," "Second Proletarian News," and "Atheist" were distributed. The two people, Kamei Ichi, a writer in the Huogong factory's work class, and Kushima Fumiko, a writer in the Fangbashi gunpowder factory, were arrested. After investigation and trial, it was found that, due to the activities of Kiyoo Motoyama, the main mountain of extreme leftism, the "no war" was promoted in the Huogong factory class, and members of the headquarters organization were contacted to plan expansion and strengthening. According to Kokumin Shinmin, Suzuki, an international proletarian youth extremist, under the instruction of a certain country, distributed extremely violent unstable documents in the name of the Central Committee of the Japanese Communist Party on September 4, and in order to contact various aspects, various propaganda leaflets were sent by the post office, with the purpose of "thoroughly obstructing Japan's military actions." Taking the retired soldiers' group as an organizational body, it caused a nationwide communist movement. The newspaper "Red Flag" was distributed in the retired soldiers' group, and secret plans were made quite vigorously. The Metropolitan Police Department discovered the matter, and Suzuki was arrested first. However, the authorities believe that the extreme leftists are making efforts to propagandize military groups and ordnance factories, and believe that the situation is serious and have begun a strict investigation.

Ferry Capsizes

Workers at Japanese Arsenal Drowned

Reuters, Tokyo, 13th. A ferry carrying about 100 workers from the naval arsenal in Kure naval port sank this morning. Most of those who fell into the water were rescued, and 24 people drowned in total. The reason for the sinking was that a large ship passed by, causing the ferry to be swayed by the waves, and several women on board were frightened and moved to one side.

China's Salt Tax is Destroyed

Still Able to Maintain Foreign Debt Credit

British Newspapers Praise Song for Finance

Reuters, London, 13th. This morning, The Times of London criticized Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen's statement that China would pay its salt debts, praising China's efforts to maintain foreign debt credit in times of special difficulty. This effort has made a good impression in London. The Nongyou Post quoted Minister Song's statement that the authorities in power are withholding salt taxes in the three eastern provinces, which hinders the National Government's ability to pay other debts, saying that although Chinese bonds have fallen and risen again, it is not surprising that they will not rise after all.

Oppose right-leaning followers of the trend and surrenderers, as well as Trotskyists from the Chen Duxiu faction, and other waning prediction factions, etc., and in China, launching a new large-scale revolutionary movement has become a meaningless and undeniable fact. The revolutionary struggle has developed particularly rapidly and significantly in recent months. The driving force of the Chinese revolution is the working class and the peasants who have been attacked by the old party, reorganized, and engaged in revolutionary struggle under the slogans of land revolution, overthrowing the authority of imperialist rule, and eliminating the counter-revolutionary Kuomintang regime (portion omitted). In the recent combat situation, it should be known that we have not yet achieved the status of revolutionizing the entire China, and the trend of labor and peasant movements has not yet been united, and the combined groups have not yet obtained the necessary strength to eliminate the system of imperialism and the Kuomintang. The revolutionary struggle of the villagers can only develop in the southern provinces. The division and mutual war between those in power and those in control have not yet completely driven them to decline and political bankruptcy, but the recent development of the situation has the following tendency: that is, if the revolutionary forces cannot occupy the entire territory of China in the near future, they must at least be able to occupy the decisive territories of various provinces. To expedite this action, the majority depends on the accuracy of the Communist Party's tactics, and first of all, it is necessary to solve the problems of consolidating the command of the Soviet movement and its future development (Document A, No. 72, see Exhibit Volume 5, pages 1 and 3). (I) A resolution of the Far Eastern Bureau on March 18, 1931, states: "The mutiny in the 20th Army of the Red Army, disarming the military academy and parts of the 12th Army, unsealing the provincial executive committee of Kaifeng, which had been ordered to be sealed by the front committee under the influence of anti-communist groups, arresting and releasing Comrade Ilsh, who was guided by the Central Executive Committee, and slogans such as 'Down with Mao Zedong, Support Zhu De, Peng Dehuai, and Wang Kelai' (all transliterations), are undoubtedly counter-revolutionary actions. These actions are prepared and implemented by class enemies and their anti-communist groups, with the aim of destroying the front lines of our party and the Red Army, seizing the rule of our party and the Red Army, so that the Nanjing counter-revolutionaries can easily eliminate the activities of the Red Army and the Soviets. The majority of party members and the entire 20th Army of the Red Army have been deceived into the criminal activities of class enemies, and cannot reduce the counter-revolutionary elements of this action in any way (portion omitted). The order sent by the Central Executive Committee to Jiangxi regarding the December incident should be used as a new supplement to this resolution, and has been copied and sent to other Soviet and military corps (Document A, No. 74, see Exhibit Volume 5, pages 21 and 24). (J) In a conversation with his comrades Moskwin, Spriid, and Xiang Zhongfa on March 27, 1931, he generally stated that his comrades Brylsky and Communar were equal to those who arrived in Jianyan Department on March 15, 1931, that wireless radios were not easy to carry, and that the Communist Party's organizational department was split. Moskwin decided to go to Hubei Tuling to recover the 20th Army (Red Army), which was currently in rebellion, and reported that the 7th Army had 5,000 people and 3,000 guns, from Guangxi to the southwest of Hunan, back to Guangxi, and then to the northwest of Guangdong. On the way to northern Guangdong, they had fought many times with the enemy and were defeated. Now, only 1,000 people and 700 guns remain (Document A, No. 41, see Exhibit Volume 5, pages 45 and 49). In all such statements, the documents contained therein either incite the military to engage in mutiny, collude with traitors, disrupt public order, or incite the people, disrupt order, or carry out propaganda of betrayal of the party and the country. None of the records are not evidence of endangering the Republic of China, and none of the actions do not constitute a criminal fact. In such a situation, the location where the documents are compiled is obviously the communist general organ established by the Third International in China. The leader who keeps the documents and presides over everything in the general organ is undoubtedly liable for criminal responsibility. Since the evidence of the crime is clear, the party then discusses the subject of the crime. According to Noulens' confession, Room 30, C, No. 49 Nanjing Road, was rented by Ericson (also known as Alison or Aenason and Aeraison), a student of his who taught German, and the key to the room was also given by Alison. The communist documents stored in the box were also owned by Alison. When Alison left Shanghai, he entrusted Noulens to take care of it on his behalf, and he did not know what the contents were, etc. Who is Alison? Where is he now? The defendant cannot produce conclusive evidence to prove it. After searching the room, in addition to a part of the N document that is considered to be harmful to the Republic of China, there are also various kinds of general plans related to the International Communist Party. The documents are of great importance to the party. Assuming that Alison is real and has indeed left Shanghai due to an event, the party entrusted the documents to a loyal comrade in his party. How could he entrust a person who has no relationship to take care of them and hand over all the stored funds and allow them to withdraw them freely? (See Gao Er Branch Court Volume 10, Exhibit Volume 4, pages 21 and 22). Moreover, according to the testimony of the witness, according to the witness Pan A Da, Room 30, C, is where this person (referring to Noulens) lives. He has been living there since December 25 last year (1930). I call him Mr. Aenason, and he gives me four yuan a month to manage the room. Ding Zhenxun testified that the rent for Room 30, No. 49 Nanjing Road, was sent to the accounting office by him (referring to Noulens) himself after we issued the notice. He calls himself Aenason, etc. (See Gao Er Branch Court Volume 103 and 106). It is found that Pan A Da and Ding Zhenxun have no grievances with the defendant, so they should not deliberately frame him. Then their testimony is naturally true. Secondly, according to the physical evidence, (Zi) the defendant ordered a set of Western clothes from the Hexing Western Clothing Store on Sichuan Road in the name of Alison on March 5, 1931, and wrote a paper order form (see Exhibit Volume 4, page 67). (Chou) Each electricity request form from the defendant's rented No. 49 Nanjing, No. 235 Sichuan Road, and No. 66 Hede Road to the electric lamp company (see Heaven No. 4 to No. 6 certificates). (Yin) Among the evidence seized in the steel box, Document A No. 18 in German has handwritten notes next to it in ink, "Adopt conspiracy rules, pay attention to mass work", "Three o'clock or four o'clock", "Six to seven people", etc. (See Exhibits Volume 1, pages 133 to 139, and Volume 3, pages 32 to 35). According to the result of the identification by the appraiser Meisheng, they are all consistent with the handwriting of the defendant's two letters to the Meifeng Bank and the head of the police (see Exhibit Volume 4, page 48, and Heaven No. 3 certificate) and are consistent. One, the writing method in each document is written to the right. Two, the size of the handwriting in each document is inconsistent. Three, the arrangement of letters is not neat and not in a straight line. The most obvious are (1) all lowercase "s" characters have no bay at the end, (2) all lowercase "i" characters are not connected to the following letters, but are connected to the preceding letters, or not connected at all, (3) all uppercase "M" characters have a high left bay and a low right bay, (4) all "C" characters have an opening at the top and are connected to the character on the left, (5) all lowercase "F" characters bend upward and then go straight down, and do not bend upward again. The remaining "A", "M", "R", etc. are also the same (see the court's volume, August 12, 1932, transcript, and Heaven No. 1 to No. 6 certificates). Although the defendant used the appraiser as a policeman as attack material, this court has carefully reviewed the appraisal result and cannot find any impropriety. The appraisal opinion can of course be adopted. According to the above-mentioned personal and physical evidence, it can be seen that Alison is Noulens, Noulens is Alison, and Room 30, C, No. 49 Nanjing Road, is indeed rented by the defendant, and there is no other person named Alison. The files seized in the room, part of the handwriting, have been proved to be written by the defendant as the defendant's property. Then all the other documents in the same place as the document and kept by the defendant, if the defendant cannot provide definite counter-evidence to prove that they are owned by others, it can be concluded that they belong to the defendant's property. Therefore, the defendant's criminal behavior can also be determined based on it. According to Gu Shunzhang, a Communist Party member who was arrested in Hankou, after being arrested, he confessed that the Third International sent several representatives to be stationed in Shanghai on a permanent basis, which is the Far East Bureau of the International. Most of these foreigners are Russians, and there are also Poles and Germans. They do not know their names and addresses. They are said to be a faction of Khablin. The director of the Far East Bureau is named Nulun (transliteration). We call him Lao Maozi. He has a wife who is very powerful. The name is unknown. In fact, she is not his wife, but another German who was sent by the Third International to monitor him in the next room. He is a military committee member named Hotinav in Russian. He knows the development of the Red Army in Xiang, E, and Gan like the back of his hand. He used to command in the Red Zone for nine months. In China, he only receives orders from Lao Maozi. He can also report directly to the International. There are seven or eight residences in Shanghai, and the precautions are very strict. I have met him twice, once on Fuxu Road and once on Yidingpan Road, both at night. The light in the room was insufficient. In addition to Lao Maozi, there was also a Chinese man surnamed Li who worked as a translator", etc. (See Gu Shunzhang's case file). According to Xiang Zhongfa, the leader of the Red Bandits who has already been executed, after being arrested, he confessed, "The head of the Eastern Department of the International Communist Party stationed in Shanghai was Miff, and he has now returned to China. He is now in charge of a Pole who claims to be from Belgium. He is currently being held in the police station in the British Concession. The name is unknown (portion omitted). The economic source is helped by the International. The Chinese Party receives 15,000 US dollars per month and distributes it to the Southern Jiangsu Bureau, the Southern Bureau, the Yangtze River Bureau, the Northern Bureau, and Manchuria" (portion omitted), etc. (See Xiang Zhongfa's case file). In addition, what is stated, such as the names of the comrades (such as Xiang Ying, Zhou Enlai, etc.) and the duties they hold, etc., and what is recorded in the documents seized from the defendant's room are mostly the same. The transliteration of Nulun in Gu Shunzhang's confession is the same as Noulens. Xiang Zhongfa said that the person in charge of the Eastern Department of the International Communist Party stationed in Shanghai claimed to be from Belgium. When the defendant in this case was arrested, he also claimed to be from Belgium. Then, the defendant is undoubtedly the leader of the International Communist Party stationed in Shanghai. Combining the above-mentioned main evidence, it is obvious that the defendant has committed the crime of endangering the Republic of China. As for the defendant's claim that he is a representative of a German company in Berlin, engaged in the import business, and teaches German and French as a profession, and did not participate in the Communist Party, etc., when asked whether he had contacted any Chinese merchants, he had no words to answer (refer to the Supreme Procuratorate Volume 99 and the court's transcript of this month's 10th). When asked about the address of the students he taught, he could not accurately point it out. It is very clear that he is using empty words and cunning defenses.

(II) Regarding the Wang Deli case, Noulens was the leader of the Far East of the Third International Communist Party stationed in Shanghai, as mentioned above. Wang Deli was the person sent by the Third International to Shanghai to monitor Noulens' work, as evidenced by the aforementioned confession of Gu Shunzhang. When Wang Deli was arrested, he had twice gone to Room 30, C, No. 49 Nanjing Road, which was rented by Noulens, and used his own key to open the door and enter the room. Among the documents seized in the room, there was a French letter that was sent from Singapore to Shanghai on May 27, 1931. The words added in ink in the letter and the French note left by the defendant to Noulens (see Exhibit Volume 4, pages 63 and 65) were written in exactly the same posture. According to the identification result of the appraiser Meisheng, all characters with circles, such as A, O, C, etc., start from the low point on the left, turn to the middle of the circle, and then go down from the middle to a suitable place to end. For example, the "A" character first circles from the lower left to the point where it turns, which is in the middle of the circle. The structures and arrangement methods of the other characters, such as I, N, R, etc., are all the same (see the court's volume, August 12, 1932, transcript, and Heaven No. 7, No. 9, No. 10, No. 15 certificates). Although the letter uses a lot of code to obscure its words, the so-called "regarding investigation work", "regarding the actions of the Labor Party", "as for checking telegrams", "and in this situation, how should it be handled", "we are organizing the Singapore office", and the defendant's added sentences "three political and specialized industrial personnel" and "have already contacted Java" are all about the Communist Party members reporting their work situation to him (see Exhibit Volume 5, page 54). Since the defendant can freely enter and exit Room 30, C, and the steel box containing the criminal documents contains the defendant's handwritten criminal letters, it is clear that the room is the joint office of the defendant and Noulens. All kinds of documents in the steel box in the room are the jointly owned objects of the defendant and Noulens. Therefore, Noulens' criminal behavior is the joint behavior of the defendant, which is undoubted. The above is enough to determine the criminal behavior of the defendants and others with more than enough evidence. Let's observe from ordinary common sense, if the defendants and others have no other plans, they should truthfully state their background when they are arrested. However, they have repeatedly changed their names and nationalities, and concealed their residences and occupations. Even the amount of deposits, departure certificates, and proofs of identity are all obscured and confused at will. Moreover, the defendant has no fixed occupation, as mentioned above, and there are four addresses where he lives, and there are eight post office boxes rented, and there are as many as four registered with the Central Wireless Telegraph. Who can believe that there are no other attempts? In addition, after Noulens was arrested and put into the car, he abandoned the long-term public bus ticket and the entrance certificate to Zhaofeng Park for fear of being recognized as Noulens Hastings, and the residence at No. 66 Hede Road (see Gao Er Branch Court Volume 98). Also, when Wang Deli entered Room 30, C, he immediately showed a flustered expression when he saw the police, and apologized, saying that he had entered the wrong room, and said that he had never seen Noulens (see Gao Er Branch Court Volume 90 to 100 and the court's volume, August 15, 1932, transcript). The defendants' fear of crime and falsehood can be seen from this. Next, it is found that the defendant Noulens came to China in March 1930, and Wang Deli came to China in July of the same year. According to the photos of the Seventh and Fifth Congress of the International Communist Party presented by the South African Consulate to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the defendants and others are all photographed in it. Then the defendants and others had already organized communist groups in 1927. Although this group is not only aimed at endangering the Republic of China, since the defendants and others are international communists, what they endanger, China, is naturally also a part of it. Moreover, after the promulgation and implementation of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China on March 1, 1931, the defendants and others continued to come to China to work, and their purpose of endangering the Republic of China is obvious.

According to the above conclusion, the defendant committed the crimes of organizing a group for the purpose of endangering the Republic of China, or inciting the military and the people, or colluding with traitors, plotting to disrupt public order, and having the practice of disrupting public order, and using words to carry out traitorous propaganda, which are in violation of Article 1, Paragraph 1, Article 3, Article 4, Article 2, Paragraph 1, Article 2, and Article 6 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. According to Article 10 of the same law and Article 42 and the latter part of Article 74 of the Criminal Law, he shall be punished according to Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. However, the defendants committed crimes before March 5, 1932, according to Article 2 of the Amnesty Ordinance promulgated on June 25 of this year, Article 79, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, the legal punishment in Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China shall be reduced by one-third, and each shall be sentenced to life imprisonment, and according to Article 106, Article 56, and Article 57, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, shall be deprived of public rights for life. The various documents and three steel boxes used or prepared for committing the crime, along with the keys, six yuan, eight jiao and four cents of silver, eight hundred and twenty-three US dollars, one hundred and fifty Japanese yen, and four envelopes containing the above-mentioned silver dollars, shall be confiscated according to Article 60, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. As for the points cited in the indictment, Article 1, Paragraph 2 and Article 5 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China, since the defendant has no facts of colluding with foreign countries to plot to disrupt public order, and has no act of purchasing and transporting military supplies for traitors, or leaking and transmitting political and military secrets to traitors, or destroying traffic, regarding this part, a judgment of innocence should be announced according to Article 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law, especially for judgment as the main text. The case was attended by the court's prosecutor Niu Jun, who performed the duties of the prosecutor. The court of appeal in this case is the Supreme Court. If the parties are not satisfied with this judgment, they should file an appeal with this court within ten days from the day after the judgment is served, with a written statement of the reasons for dissatisfaction. August 19, 1932, Criminal First Tribunal of the Jiangsu High Court, Presiding Judge Li Mian, Judge Lin Zhezhang, Judge Yin Rixu.

The Commander of the 27th Division

Gao Shixun Dismissed

Because of Retreating and Abandoning Defense Lines

Still Subject to Investigation After Dismissal

Nanchang Correspondence, Around the beginning of last month, in addition to the pseudo-fourth army corps guarding the old nest, the various units of Niu Mao, Peng Lin (Biao), Ji (Zhentong), and Luo (Binghui), the first, third, and fifth pseudo-army corps, invaded the north of Yihuang and Le'an from Ningdu and Yongfeng. At that time, Li Songkun's unit of the 25th Division of Sun Lianzhong's department was stationed in Le'an, Gao Shixun's unit of the 27th Division was stationed in Yihuang, and Guan Shuren's cavalry division was stationed in Chongren, bearing the brunt of the bandit impact. By the middle of the month, the vanguard team of the bandits, Xiao Ke's unit of the fifth pseudo-division, first captured Le'an, and Yihuang was shaken. When Peng Fei's main force arrived in Yicheng, Gao Shixun claimed that he was outnumbered and wanted to retreat. At that time, Sun received He Yingqin's order and immediately used the telephone from Fuzhou to instruct Gao to defend Yihuang to the death. However, the battle did not last a day. Gao retreated with the entire division on the 20th, and Yihuang was captured by the bandits at 2:00 am on the 21st. The bandits occupied it for ten days, losing more than a million. The people of Yi are gnashing their teeth. When Gao withdrew from the county seat of Yi Le, although the losses were more than two regiments, there were still three or four thousand people. He could have set up defenses in the Hangbu Qiuxi area on the border of Linchuan and Yihuang to protect Fuzhou. However, Gao not only lost Yicheng, but also abandoned the important Longgudu pass without defending it, and retreated into Linchuan County, allowing the Red Bandits to drive straight in and approach Linchuan, shaking the provincial capital. At that time, He Yingqin was in Lushan to retain President Wang. After receiving the news, he rushed back to Nanchang and ordered the Chen Cheng and Wu Qiewei armies to intercept the bandits from Chong. Zhou Hunyuan's division rushed to Fuzhou overnight, and Fuzhou was able to turn the tide. Now He Yingqin believed that Gao Shixun was timid and abandoned the defense area, so he urgently telegraphed Hankou to report to Chairman Jiang and asked him to dismiss Gao and investigate him. He then received a telegram approving it. He then telegraphed Gao Shixun on the 10th to remove him from the positions of army commander and division commander and await investigation to uphold military discipline (11th).

Zhang Zongchang's Coffin Transported From Ji to Ping

Jinan Correspondence, After Zhang Zongchang was assassinated in Jinan, Han Fuqu, the chairman of the provincial government, purchased a coffin for his body. It was embalmed in Jinan Hospital and transported to the Anhui Township Ancestral Hall on Wanxin Street in Anhui on the 4th to await his family members to come. At first, some of his family members advocated opening a memorial service in Jinan and then transporting the coffin back to his hometown of Yexian for burial in his ancestral tomb. Later, due to various reasons, he could not be buried and it was decided to transport him to Beiping. Zhang's mother sent Wang Jinyu, the former director of Zhang Chengqi, to Jinan to handle this matter. Wang arrived in Jinan yesterday morning but failed to meet Chairman Han. He went to the provincial government again this morning and was met by Han Wenxiu, the adjutant general, on behalf of Han. Wang Jinyu stated his intention to transport the coffin back to Ping. Han agreed to order the station to prepare a car for him. In the afternoon, Guan Shilian, the director of the headquarters' station office, prepared a forty-ton flat Han Line No. 4241 iron shed car and decided to attach it to the Tianjin-Pukou Line train No. 10 heading north to Ping. Most of Zhang's old subordinates had already left Jinan. Only Wang Jinyu and Zhang's relatives who came with Wang were in Jinan to take care of him. Zhang's coffin was moved out of the Anhui Township Ancestral Hall at 2:00 pm and transported by a Duling car. It arrived at the station at 2:30 pm. The coffin was covered with yellow cloth and transported onto the iron shed car. His relatives spread reed mats on the car and sat and lay beside the coffin to guard it. The situation was extremely miserable. Zhang was a hero for half his life and was watched by the whole country. When Zhang went to Qingdao from Jinan for inspection in the 16th year, he was escorted by clouds of people. The Jiaoji Road once opened seven special trains for him. This time, he revisited Jinan. Although it was not the same as the previous situation, there were still many old friends who welcomed and sent him off. Today, his remains are transported north, and no one is sending him off. Only Wang Jinyu is taking care of him. It is also sad. According to Wang Jinyu, Zhang's family members said that no one lives in their home in Yexian, so it is very inconvenient to transport the coffin back for burial. There is a newly purchased piece of land in Nanyuan in Ping, so it was decided to temporarily bury it there. The car left Jinan at 3:00 pm and will arrive in Ping tomorrow.

According to Zhang Zongchang, he served as the Shandong Military Affairs Director of Rehabilitation in the 14th year and arrived in Jinan on May 7 of that year. In the 17th year, the Northern Expeditionary Army advanced, and Zhang withdrew from Jinan on the evening of April 30. He was in Shandong for two years and ten months, and then drifted to Japan and Dalian. He returned to Beiping last year. On the morning of September 2 of this year, he arrived in Jinan from Ping at 9:00 am and died at the station at 6:30 pm the next afternoon. Eight days after his death (the 11th), the coffin left Jinan and was transported to Ping. One coffin was attached to him and everything was done. The end of the warlord is also sad (11th).

Western Journey Notes (21)

(3) The coal seam is quite flat and thick, six feet, with soil above the coal seam, no support required.

(4) The selling price of lump coal is one dime per hundred catties delivered at the wellhead, fine coal has no market.

(5) The coal quality is bituminous coal, inferior to that of Tongguan. Charcoal easily soils hands, and it is the same geological era (Jurassic) as the Yishicun coal mine. According to the chemical analysis of the average composition of the Yishicun bituminous coal sample by the Central Geological Research Institute, the water content is 6.36, ash content 36.2, volatile matter 12.35, fixed carbon 45.08, and calorific value 5067.41.

Traveling west from Yaoxian Village for another eight or nine li is Cuijia Gou. Numerous earthen kilns are lined up there, all excavated along the outcrops at the foot of the mountain. Mining has been suspended because there is no market for the coal. I went down the well to inspect, and the situation is as follows:

(1) A vertical shaft with a diameter of four feet and a depth of fifty zhang, without supports, leads directly to the inclined shaft bottom's level tunnel for ventilation.

(1) The inclined shaft is six feet high and three and a half feet wide, with an inclination of about thirty degrees, facing northwest twenty degrees, with an inclined depth of more than fifty zhang.

(3) The coal seam is eight to ten feet thick. According to the miners, it can be as thick as thirty feet. The mining tunnel is six feet high, leaving more than two feet of coal at the top. The coal seam is topped with soil and bottomed with shale, trending northeast-southwest, dipping northwest, quite flat, some up to ten degrees. The coal quality is the same as the coal in Yaoxian Village, half lump and half fine. Coal samples have been collected and are awaiting chemical analysis. There is gas in the coal seam that can spontaneously ignite. When it catches fire, it is immediately filled with stones and sealed with mud. Now, the abandoned kilns are due to fire or water.

(4) The selling price is four to five dimes per kǔai (approximately 240 to 300 catties). Nearby farmers take coal mining as a side business, so they stop during the busy farming season and start during the slack season.

After viewing the Cuijia Gou earthen kilns, I returned to Ping. At 11:00 AM, I arrived at Jiao Town. A soldier sent by Yijun was suffering from tiger fever. The patrol officer also claimed to be sick. All three returned to the county. Two militiamen were sent by District Chief Yan to accompany me to Qilipu. I left Jiao at around 2:00 PM. The original journey was only ninety li, but for safety reasons, I detoured through Shancha, adding thirty li. That night, I stayed at Liu Jia Zhuang Ke, fifty li northeast of Jiao Town. The lodging was an earthen cave, fifteen feet wide and about twenty feet deep. The inner end was a stable, and the entrance was an earthen kiln. I slept on the earthen pit. The village chief made noodles with wheat flour, with vinegar, black salt, and spicy sauce, plus a bowl of bean pods. It was said that six families had to pool together to get this. The villagers are underfed and poorly clothed, yet they treated me like a guest, which is touching. On the 24th, I set off at 7:30 AM and headed northeast towards Qilipu. Along the way, I passed through Shancha and Baiziqiao Village, and militiamen guided me section by section. At 5:00 PM, I arrived at my destination and inspected the Zhangjiawan and Houziping coal mines. The situation is described below:

(A) Zhangjiawan Coal Mine is about two li southeast of Qilipu. The coal seam is four feet thick, trends north-south, and dips quite flat. The coal price is three dimes per hundred catties. The geological era is Jurassic. The coal quality is comparable to that of the Cuijia Gou area. Mining has been suspended due to slow sales.

(B) Houziping Coal Mine

(1) Location: Two li southwest of Qilipu, 93 li from Yijun. (2) The coal seam is seven or eight feet thick, trending northeast-southwest, and dipping quite flat. The roof is sandstone, and the floor is one inch thick shale. There is still a coal seam under the rock, but the thickness is unknown because it has not been mined. The coal quality is bituminous and contains a lot of sulfur iron. It is the same geological era as the Zhangjiawan Coal Mine. The coal seam contains a lot of shale, and the ash content seems high.

(3) The level tunnel is opened northeast from the coal seam outcrop. There are three level tunnels, one for coal, one for water, and one for ventilation. The coal-producing level tunnel is excavated at 30 degrees southeast, the tunnel is three feet high and wide, and the tunnel is 1,700 steps long (five feet per step).

(4) Coal is mined by opening level tunnels in the direction of the coal seam and dipping at 1,700 steps in the level tunnel. Coal is mined when it is seen, without any fixed method. Coal pillars are not left, and very little wood is used. Single logs are only used for support in dangerous places. When the coal is finished, the wood is taken out and moved elsewhere. Each miner can produce 700 to 800 catties of coal. The town stipulates that each miner who pulls coal must produce five carts of coal, each cart containing 200 to 260 catties of coal. However, because the coal seam often contains shale up to two feet thick, coal mining often cannot meet the specified amount. The coal cart is made of wood, five feet long, one and a half feet wide, and five inches high, with iron wheels on the bottom.

(5) Ventilation is done with wooden bellows blowing air into the tunnel, two people per shift, four people day and night.

(6) Lighting is done with sesame oil lamps, four to six ounces of oil per shift, and the oil price is five dimes per catty.

(7) Workers' treatment and living conditions: Diggers, pullers, handymen (i.e., odd-job men), and wind workers earn about three dimes per day. Lamp oil and tools are supplied by the mine owner. Food is provided by themselves, costing about two dimes per person per day. Each shift works ten hours. Commodity prices are as follows:

Millet 1 dime 5 cents per liter (weighing 3 catties)

Corn 5 cents per liter (weighing 3 catties)

Rice 1 dime 8 cents per liter (weighing 3 and a half catties)

Local flour 1 dime 8 cents per liter (weighing 3 and a half catties)

Vegetables 1 cent per catty

Pork 2 dimes per catty

Coarse cloth 5 cents per foot

(8) The selling price of bituminous coal delivered on the mine is four dimes per hundred catties, and it has been sold for six dimes when prices rise.

(9) There are more than 20 investors in the mine. After seeing the coal, they mine and sell it separately. Approximately three to five companies mine together in one place. The mined coal is divided equally among the companies, stored separately, and sold by each company.

On the evening of the 24th, I stayed at the Qilipu District Office. Tiger fever is prevalent in the town. I only ate three king corn and four eggs. On the morning of the 25th, at 6:30 AM, I left Qilipu and headed northeast to Fu County. District Chief Jiang sent two militiamen to escort me. That day, I traveled eighty li and stayed at Siyuan Town. The place is in the deep mountains, with only two shops and no other residents. I was quite wary and could not sleep. At 3:30 AM, I suddenly heard knocking on the door. I woke up in surprise and saw three passing merchants. We sat together to wait for dawn and left at six o'clock. That day (the 26th), I traveled sixty li and arrived at Fu County at 3:00 PM. From Qilipu to Fu, some say ninety li, some say one hundred li, and some say one hundred and twenty li, but in the end, I traveled as much as one hundred and forty li and took as long as two days. This was because the mountain roads were rugged (passing through eight deep valleys and eight high mountains) and I took the wrong route.

Other mining conditions heard along the way and in Fu County are as follows:

(1) There is a coal mine in Liushu Village, fifty li northwest of Central County.

(2) The Hulugou Coal Mine, ten li west of Qilipu, has a coal seam more than three feet thick.

(3) The coal kilns of the Guojia Ta Coal Mine, thirteen or fourteen li northwest of Siping Town, are by the river.

In Fu County, I met Mr. Xie Jiarong, Yang Gongzhao, and Hu Bosu from the Peiping Geological Survey Institute. They said that they had been to the Niuwuzhen coal mine in Zhangchuanyi for investigation, and the thickness was less than two feet, so it was not very valuable. On the 27th, I went to Ganquan with Mr. Xie. Mr. Xie and others then went to Yanchang from Ganquan via a small road. On the 28th, I arrived in Fushi and reunited with the team. Meeting everyone, we talked happily, and the experiences we had on each road made our hearts feel a lot more comfortable. (Sent from Fushi on August 28)

Local Correspondence Songjiang

Song County's Autumn Harvest is Abundant. The rice and cotton harvests in the county's various townships have all been abundant. However, due to the decline in rice prices, farmers, even if they harvest more, have a sense of "cheap grain hurts farmers".

Verifying and Reporting Business Tax

The director of the Business Tax Bureau here, Jinde, recently sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, asking it to advise various trade associations to persuade all businesses to verify and report their declaration forms. Only about one-tenth of those who have filled out the forms have submitted them to the bureau. Now that the autumn collection period is approaching, an investigation needs to be launched urgently, and it is hoped that assistance will be given in filling out the forms so that the work can proceed smoothly.

Poison Pills Invade Song Territory

Since red pills have become popular in various counties, they have been secretly sold in Punan and the northeastern townships of the county, and quite a few people have become addicted to this habit. It is said that, except for the urban area, there is probably no place in this area where red pills have not been imported.

Seawall Project Gradually Under Construction

Since Xu Baikui, director of the Songjiang section of the Jiangnan Seawall Project, took office, he has been actively planning. The new post-disaster projects include the second section of 37 zhang pile stone project, the third section of 220 zhang concrete supplementary project, and the fourth section of 160 zhang riprap project. All of them started construction in June of this year and were completed on schedule by the 10th of this month. As for the old seawall of 136 zhang in the second section, which has been in disrepair for many years, Director Xu has repeatedly requested the Provincial Department of Construction and the Jiangnan Seawall Committee to find ways to allocate funds for early construction. The Provincial Department of Construction and the Jiangnan Seawall Committee also recognized that this section was indeed dangerous and tried to allocate funds as soon as possible. It is said that as soon as the committee allocates wood and stone materials, Director Xu will raise funds as soon as possible for emergency repairs and then gradually expand them based on economic strength to achieve perfection.

Taicang

Kunxing Steamer Dispute. This county's transportation business has made little progress in the past ten years. It is quite inconvenient to travel between Shanghai and Taicang. In June last year, a county resident founded a Kunxing steamer, using the latest German-style Stobick engine, which was small, stable, and fast, making it convenient for passengers. This spring, when the January 28th Incident occurred, the ship assisted the army in carrying out transportation work and was burned down in Weiting in March. After the war, the shipowner repaired it and restored it to its former appearance. However, Mao Tigan, the district chief of the eighth district of Shuangfeng, filed a report with the Construction Department to ban the ship, saying that it hindered the dike bank. However, when the ship was founded last year, it had already been approved by the administrative authorities and construction bureaus of Kunshan and Taicang counties. Therefore, it is now presenting the facts to the Construction Department, stating that it does not hinder farmland and requesting legal protection.

Changshu

County Principal Beaten. Since Principal Sang Xin took over the county's junior high school, classes have not yet officially started due to strong opposition from the students. On the 12th, Principal Sang Xin went to the school again and planned to start classes. However, because the notice to the parents of the former students involved the instigation of the old teachers, they went to the principal's office to question him. Sang had nothing to say. At that time, the students felt empathy and clamored. Some students flashed out from the crowd and beat Principal Sang once, then ran away. Sang asked after turning around, but he didn't know where they went. Then he gathered the students and held a memorial week in the dining hall. The students threw small stones, sand, bamboo pieces, and other things at Principal Sang Xin. When the newly appointed teachers saw this, they dispersed one after another. Principal Sang also walked out of the school, but the school gate was guarded by students and he was not allowed to leave. Sang escaped from the back door. The students in the school destroyed the glass and other items in the principal's office. Now the school affairs are suspended, pending the authorities' disposal.

The Department Orders a Secret Investigation of the Public Security Bureau Chief's Case. Pan Zhengfen, the district chief of the twelfth district of this county, was ordered to be transferred. When he was preparing the handover documents, the township chiefs of the district found that the finances were not in order and believed that the district chief had committed corruption. They immediately filed a complaint with the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments. Later, the Finance Department ordered the county to reply. Before long, the township chiefs of the district, Zhao Menghao, Wang Yinglong, etc., went to the city for business and stayed at the Daxin Hotel. It is not known why District Chief Pan reported it to the Public Security Bureau and arrested Wang Yinglong and others, accusing them of destroying the public office. Although they were explained later, they were released on bail. However, the township chiefs and others believed that District Chief Pan was holding a grudge, and the Public Security Bureau Chief Yin had arbitrarily arrested good people. They continued to file a complaint with the Civil Affairs Department and also published a warning to Bureau Chief Yin in the newspaper. The Civil Affairs Department specially sent a commissioner, Zhao Jun, to Changshu for a secret investigation. It was quite secret beforehand. Later, it was learned that Zhao had gone to the county government to investigate and summoned Bureau Chief Yin and Sun Yao, the chief of the Public Security Branch of the twelfth district, for questioning. According to Zhao, he had found some clues and returned to the province on the 11th to report his findings.

Verdict on the Love Case of Male and Female Students. Gu Weian from Funing, who was studying at Shanghai Law School, had an affair with Zhao Yueying, a woman from Changzhou, three years ago. This summer, he met Lei Peijing, the niece of the Lei Junjin, a giant family from Songjiang, who was studying at a girls' school in Shanghai, and they developed a relationship. They once lived together at No. 59 Dongfang Apartment in Shanghai. Last month, they came to Suzhou and stayed at No. 31 Central Hotel. Zhao Yueying found out and rushed to negotiate, resulting in a fierce fight. They were arrested by the police and sent to the local court. Gu Weian was detained, and the two women, Zhao and Lei, were ordered to return. Wuxi

Robbing Farmers and Arresting Them on the Spot. Shen Qiao'er, a farmer from Liu Shen Lane in the seventh district of the county (Huai Shang City), about two li from Zhangjingqiao, made a living by farming and had some savings. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 AM the night before, more than 20 robbers suddenly came, armed with iron rods, flashlights, and other weapons. They rushed in, first tied up the victims Shen Qiao'er, his son Wenmei, and daughter-in-law Chen with ropes, and forced them to tell where the silver was hidden. Then, they looted extensively. At that time, the neighbors heard the alarm and immediately rang the gong to warn the police. At the same time, the neighbors rushed to Zhangjingqiao to report to the defense regiment. After receiving the report, Gu Weijing, the head of the regiment, immediately led six members to arrest the robbers. Unexpectedly, the robbers had already heard the news and escaped. Only one robber, Jiang Xiqi, was captured on the spot. At the same time, the defense regiment saw a thief escaping into the river and bravely chased and captured him. According to the confession, his name was Tang Sanbao. Regiment Leader Gu immediately brought the two captured thieves back to the regiment and interrogated them severely. The thieves claimed that they both had families, and there were still old mothers and wives. This time, they were forced to take the risk because of the difficulty of making a living and were gathered by Tang Heshang, etc. Yesterday (the 13th), they prepared a document and transferred them to the county government for legal action.

County Delegates Confuse the Party Certificate Issue. The Fourth County Congress was held on the 10th to elect executive and supervisory committee members, which has been completed. On the 11th, Provincial Supervisor Zhang Gongren summoned the newly elected executive and supervisory committee members for a conversation and then returned to the province. However, at the time of the election, Xu Peiqi, a delegate from the first branch of the fourth district, did not submit the party certificate for inspection. A party member, Wu Zhong, reported that Xu Peiqi had stated to the district party department that it had been lost, and at the first congress, he submitted a vague party certificate to the credential examination committee. Later, it was learned that he had confused it with Liu Fobao's party certificate. During the election, executive committee members Xue Chan and Wu Fengnian certified it, and Supervisor Zhang issued the ballot. It was stated that if it was found that it was confused, he would be subject to the most severe party discipline. Yesterday (the 11th), Xu Peiqi took out the party certificate, which was inspected by Zhang and found to have no number and a blurry photo, obviously fraudulent. Zhang then took it to the province for a decision on the method. Party member Wu Zhong and Liu Fobao also presented the situation of Xu Peiqi and Xu Er'ying (Peiqi's father), the standing committee member of the fourth district party department, to Zhang, requesting the provincial party department to severely punish them.

Nantong

Regulations on Restricted Areas for Grass Burning. The salt pans and stoves in the Huainan area have fixed area for storing grass to burn. However, salt pan workers are often caught because they do not understand the restrictions, and there are also anti-smuggling personnel who deliberately make things difficult and cause more trouble. The Department of Industry has now submitted a request to the provincial government, which has been forwarded to the Ministry of Finance, to appropriately open up the restricted area for grass burning in Huainan. The restricted area is specified as Lusi Field, Yu Dong Zheng Field, and Yu Xi Bin Field in Tong County. The punishment for private grass cases is: (1) Grass and firewood carried by vehicles or boats, or on shoulders, weighing less than 100 catties, will be exempted from interception. (2) Those who traffic in private grass weighing more than 100 catties and less than 2,000 catties will have the grass and firewood seized. (3) Those who traffic in private grass weighing more than 2,000 catties will have the grass and firewood and the vehicles, boats, and cattle used to transport them confiscated.

The New Cotton Market in Tongruhai is Prosperous. The new cotton in Tongruhai County has entered the market. The total output this year is estimated to be around 1.5 million dan. In recent days, cotton merchants from Shanghai, Wuxi, and other ports have flocked to the market, and the market is booming. Skin cotton is 45 yuan per dan and seed cotton is 16 yuan.

Gaoyou

筹办地方银行 The Financing of Local Banks in this county has always relied on the Zhenjiang bank for transfer, and in recent years, due to the situation, banks and money houses have been taking a contractionary approach. In addition, the floods last year and the impact of the Shanghai incident have made funds extremely tight. The town banks and money houses only accept deposits and do not make loans, causing more than a dozen money houses in this county to go out of business one after another. Only Hengxiang Yifeng remains, which has greatly affected various industries and prevented them from operating. Seeing this, local gentry Lu Bochun, in order to seek relief, united with merchants Liu Jiansan and others to establish a local bank with a capital of 100,000 yuan, and issued local paper currency.

Bandits from Yinjia Village Resist Arrest. The Yinjia Village Defense Regiment in the fifth district of the county has been patrolling every night since the Chen family was robbed in the village. At about 11 p.m. the night before, more than ten bandits, each holding guns, intended to rob. They were spotted by the defense regiment, who went forward to interrogate them. Unexpectedly, the bandits suddenly opened fire. After a fierce battle for half an hour, the bandits were unable to hold out and began to swim east to escape.

Special Feature on Education News.

Problems of Moral Education in Elementary Schools (Part 1) by Wu Zengjie

Elementary education should not only enable children to acquire knowledge and skills, but also teach them how to conduct themselves. The importance of moral education in elementary schools is undeniable. Recently, the Ministry of Education held a meeting of the Curriculum Enrollment Committee, and the most noteworthy revision of the elementary school curriculum was the establishment of "Civic Training" to implement "Direct Moral Education." The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education promulgated a plan for the integration of moral and academic education in primary and secondary schools a few days ago. The Fujian Provincial Department of Education convened a provincial conference on moral education for primary and secondary schools during the summer vacation this year, and offered a course on "Elementary School Moral Education" at the summer school organized by the department, with the author serving as a lecturer. The emphasis placed on children's training by educational administrative authorities is evident.

Let us examine the current implementation of moral education in general elementary schools, which mainly involves the following:

(1) Children's Self-Government Organizations: Children's self-governing bodies, where students elect leaders to take on responsibilities.

(2) Training Week: The moral education department or moral education committee formulates implementation measures and conducts them separately.

(3) Rewards and Punishments: Students with good behavior are given rewards, while those with bad behavior are arbitrarily punished by teachers.

(4) Speeches: The principal, director of moral education, or homeroom guidance teacher gives oral admonitions to students during public gatherings, grade meetings, or evening meetings.

(5) Posting Slogans: Writing slogans using idioms, proverbs, and maxims and posting them in classrooms, corridors, or public places.

On the surface, these methods seem very sound. Those who do not think deeply may believe that this is all there is to moral education for elementary school students. However, if you think carefully, these methods have flaws and problems that are worth studying. Now, I will raise several issues that require urgent attention and discuss them with colleagues in the field of elementary education. (1) How to Formulate Moral Education Articles: Moral education articles are the basis for examining the effectiveness of moral education and for implementing it. They are not only useful for teachers, but also allow students to reflect on themselves at any time. Parents who want to know about their children's situation at school can simply see which articles of the code they are able to follow. However, compiling the articles should not be done casually. First, one must consider local conditions. Shortcomings in the local area should be given special attention. Second, one must consider the school's situation. The specific shortcomings of the students at the school should be given more training, and more articles should be listed accordingly. Therefore, articles suitable for elementary schools in Place A may not be suitable for Place B. The articles of elementary schools in the same place may not be completely interchangeable. The most important thing to note is that the articles for rural elementary schools and urban elementary schools should be different.

Important News

Ministry of Education Orders All Schools to Commemorate the

September 18th National Crisis

Meeting to Be Held at 9 AM

To Discuss Methods of Saving the Nation

Nanjing, 13th—Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua telegraphed all national colleges and universities and provincial and municipal education departments, stating: "The first anniversary of the September 18th National Crisis is approaching. The unprecedented humiliation is unforgettable. The disaster is still ongoing, like a raging fire. All Chinese people are in pain and indignation every day, and on this day in particular, we should actively encourage each other to be leaders in all circles. Therefore, I order all schools at all levels across the country to convene all students at 9 AM on that day to hold a commemoration on campus, suspend the usual weekly holidays, give lectures on the facts of national humiliation, and discuss methods of saving the nation, in order to demonstrate the spirit of enduring hardship and preparing to wipe out the national humiliation. I order you to strictly comply and instruct your subordinates to do the same."

Zhu Jingnong Assumes Office as Director of the Hunan Provincial Department of Education

Huang Guoluo and Wang Linggen were appointed as secretaries. There were few other changes. Local News

County Education Bureau

Held a Meeting of Social Education Organizations Yesterday

The Shanghai County Education Bureau convened the first meeting of social education organizations for this semester yesterday morning. Attendees included Jin Zuobin, Zhang You, Zhang Yi, Yao Wenlai, Yang Huiming, Zheng Shaoyuan, and Sun Tingfang. The Tangwan People's Education Center was absent. Yang Huiming chaired the meeting, and Zheng Shaoyuan recorded the minutes. Reported Items: (1) All organizations must submit daily work reports to the bureau by the 3rd of next month. (2) Provisional regulations for the assessment of leading personnel in social education organizations promulgated by the provincial government. (3) Concrete plans for promoting people's schools within three years promulgated by the provincial government. (4) A letter from the Provincial Nanjing People's Education Center notifying the date of the provincial agricultural exhibition. Discussion Items: (1) Determining the locations of people's schools for this term. It was decided that: "First People's Education District": First People's School, within Shouhua Elementary School, Grade 1; Second People's School, Huangjiatang, Grade 1; Third People's School, within Yinghu Elementary School, Grade 1. "Second People's Education District": First People's School, within Shuangxi Elementary School, Grade 1; Second People's School, within Wu Jing Elementary School, Grade 1; Third People's School, within Hua Jing Elementary School, Grade 1; Fourth People's School, within Xu Jing Elementary School, Grade 1. "Third People's Education District": First People's School, Beiqiao Tea Garden, Grade 1; Second People's School, Zhao Jia Yan, Grade 2. "Fourth People's Education District": First People's School, Dongming Elementary School, Grade 1; Second People's School, within Wuquan Elementary School, Grade 1; Third People's School, within Fang Er Elementary School, Grade 1. "Fifth People's Education District": First People's School, within Chenxing Elementary School, Grade 1; Second People's School, within Tangkou Elementary School, Grade 1; Third People's School, within San Gui Elementary School, Grade 1. "Sixth People's Education District": First People's School, Shen Jingbang, Grade 2; Second People's School, within Qingdeng Elementary School, Grade 1. (2) Deciding on textbooks for people's schools. It was decided to use the World Book Company's "People's Reader." (3) How to organize school equipment for people's schools. It was decided that each social education organization should collect and organize the equipment. If there are not enough kerosene lamps, insurance lamps should be added. (4) Date of the first meeting of people's school principals. It was decided to hold it on September 18th. (5) Calligraphy teaching in people's schools. It was decided to use pencils and newspapers for copying in the first month, and then use ink brushes for practice after the second month. (6) Stipulating the subjects and weekly class hours for each people's school. It was decided to have six periods of Mandarin Chinese per week (270 minutes), three periods of arithmetic (130 minutes), two periods of general knowledge (90 minutes), and one period of recreation (45 minutes). (7) Opening date for people's schools. It was decided to open on September 20th. The meeting adjourned.
