Recent News from the Veterinary Specialty School

Last year, Cai Wuji, Wang Zhaoji, Cheng Shaojiong, and Chen Shunyun organized the Veterinary Education Promotion Association and established the Veterinary Specialty School at the China Vocational Education Society. Veterinary doctors who had studied in Europe and America, such as Fen Wuji, Wang Zhaoji, Cheng Shaojiong, and Chen Shunyun, served as professors. There were more than 40 students. It has been a year since the school opened, and it has been registered with the Ministry of Education. All important subjects, such as anatomy, pharmacology, internal medicine, surgery, infectious diseases, parasitology, diagnostic techniques, bacteriology, immunology, blood serum production, meat inspection, animal husbandry, and chicken farming, have been thoroughly studied. Last year, cattle plague was prevalent in Sichuan, Qinghai, and other provinces, and hundreds of thousands of cattle died of the disease, which aroused the attention of the people of the country. This summer, the academic courses have come to an end. In order to implement the theories learned, students were divided into five groups from September 1st and sent to the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Health Bureau, Serum Production Institute, Minsheng Chicken Farm, and Shengsheng Milk Company for internships. After the internships, they will be assigned to work in various places. The Qinghai Provincial Government, Nantong University, Fuzhou, and Yunnan Agricultural and Forestry Schools have all sent letters to hire graduates from the school. If you wish to contact the school, please write directly to Cai Wuji at the Commodity Inspection Bureau on Museum Road in Shanghai or Wang Zhaoji at the Shanghai Health Bureau.

Opening of the Xinhua Art College

The Xinhua Art College in this city held its autumn opening ceremony yesterday morning. More than 300 faculty and students attended. Principal Xu gave an opening speech and reported on the recent purchase of the school site and the planning of the construction of the school building with the school directors. The directors have agreed to start construction in the shortest possible time, and the original school building will be used for the normal school. Dean Wang and Director Yu reported on the improvement of school affairs and education, and the plan to renovate the school gate and construct the campus. The faculty members all gave sincere speeches.

Sports

Grass Court Tennis Open Doubles

Lin Qiu Wins Replay Rights

Defeats Canavero Jiang Daozhang Yesterday

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai played against Canavero and Jiang Daozhang yesterday in the second week of the Grass Court Tennis Association Open Doubles at the China Tennis Court. Lin and Qiu eliminated Canavero and Jiang in straight sets to win the replay rights. The atmosphere of the match was tense, especially in the final set. The results are listed below:

Lin Baohua Qiu Feihai 6-3 6-3 9-7 Canavero Jiang Daozhang

Canavero and Jiang Unable to Maintain Balance

In the first and second sets, the opening situation was very even. In the first set, Lin won the first game by serving, and Canavero et al. took it back. Then it was 2-2 and 3-3. After that, they suddenly lost three games in a row and lost the first set. The second set was also done in the same way. Canavero and Jiang took a 3-2 lead and lost four games in a row, losing another set. It was not until the third set that the situation changed.

Canavero's Craftiness is Delightful

Canavero, the veteran who once held the Shanghai Doubles Championship, his craftiness in delivering the ball is probably unparalleled at sea. It is a pity that his physical strength is not enough, so he has to retreat behind the young talents. In the third set, Canavero often flew a high ball full of flexibility over Lin Qiu, forcing them to retreat to the baseline and then come online to kill it. Lin Qiu was often embarrassed by this and formed the situation in the third set.

The Competition in the Third Set Was Spectacular

The third set was a difficult to separate situation. Each side won a game. After reaching 7-7, Lin Qiu won two more games to determine the victory. The competition was also very spectacular. Canavero and Jiang used high balls to repel the enemy and launched a fierce pressure kill, and the mutual pounce shots of both sides in the half court were also one of the highlights. It is a pity that Canavero's backhand has no fighting power, and Jiang's shot is often in the net, so although they often take the lead with a score of 3-1, they ultimately fail.

The audience's disturbance affects the game. When the third set was at the point where the two sides were competing for 4-4, the baseball field and football field ended, so thousands of people poured in, causing great chaos and surrounding the court on the left, right, front, and back. The game was stopped for a moment. According to Canavero's post-match talk, he could have reversed the defeat in this game, but unfortunately it was lost due to the obstruction of the rioters. He was very frustrated and hoped that the authorities would take measures to improve management and avoid leaving a bad impression on foreigners.

Tung Wah and Lincoln Draw

| The Performance Was Very Exciting |

| Will Compete Again Tomorrow |

The Tung Wah football team played a friendly match with the Lincoln team at the China Baseball Stadium yesterday. This was the beginning of the winter football competition. In the second half, Tung Wah's lineup was adjusted, and its strength was enhanced, and it scored two goals in a row, taking the lead. Later, Lincoln scored another goal, and the score ended in a 3-3 draw.

Tung Wah's Strength is Not Satisfactory - Tung Wah's formation was scattered in the first half, making it difficult to attack and defend, and there were hidden dangers everywhere. There was a risk of losing the defense from time to time. The forwards were particularly weak and had few opportunities to advance. Local News

Municipal Government Circular to All Agencies

Solemnly Commemorate the National Humiliation

Stop Entertainment on September 18th

Suspend Work and Silently Vow to Eradicate National Humiliation

The anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation is fast approaching. Business associations and other groups in this city are actively preparing for a commemorative meeting. A resolution has been passed during preparatory meetings to hold the event at the Xiaoximen Juvenile Propaganda Corps at 9:00 AM on September 18th. The Municipal Government, upon receiving an order from the Executive Yuan, issued instructions to its subordinate agencies yesterday, stating that they must comply. The Executive Yuan’s instructions stated that the Central Executive Committee's Secretariat's document No. 10189 stated that, as the anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation is imminent, all commemorative measures, as decided by the Central Committee's 35th Standing Committee Meeting, stipulate that all entertainment should be suspended nationwide on that day. All party members, civil servants, military and police personnel, agencies, schools, households, factories, and shops should suspend work for five minutes at 11:00 AM, stand in silence to vow to eradicate national humiliation, and express deep condolences to the compatriots who died in the Northeast and Shanghai battles. In addition to circulating this information, this letter is specially issued for your reference, requesting that you circulate it to all your subordinates for compliance. Furthermore, the letter instructs the Municipal Government to immediately comply and circulate this to all subordinates for compliance. In addition to issuing separate directives, this order is issued for the Bureau to comply and instruct all subordinates to comply with this order.

Zhang Qun Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Delivers Chiang's Condolences for Wang Jingwei's Illness

Urges Early Return to Nanjing to Preside Over Central Affairs

Wang's Blood Pressure is High, Making a Temporary Return to Nanjing Difficult

Mr. Wang Jingwei's stay in Shanghai due to illness has caused speculation from all sides. Yesterday morning, Central Committee member Zhang Qun, bearing the orders of Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing to meet with Mr. Wang, express condolences for his illness, and urge him to return to Nanjing as soon as possible to preside over central affairs. State Council Chairman Lin Sen and Acting Premier Song Ziwen also visited Mr. Wang together yesterday afternoon. According to Chairman Lin, Mr. Wang's fever has increased, making a temporary return to Nanjing difficult. Details of each situation are recorded below.

Zhang Qun's Remarks: Central Committee member Zhang Qun, previously奉(feng)奉(feng) on orders from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to go to Peiping for negotiations, returned to Wuhan on the 9th of this month to report on his mission. He left Wuhan on the 10th and returned to Nanjing, arriving in Shanghai by overnight train at 8:10 AM yesterday morning, and went directly to his private residence to rest. According to Mr. Zhang's remarks to reporters at the North Station, after the Pacification Commissioner's Office in North China was abolished and reorganized into the Military Affairs Commission, it has now begun operations. All generals have returned to their defense posts. In the future, they will resolutely adhere to the government's declaration and unite as one to deal with foreign affairs. The rumors that Zhang Xueliang is replacing Chairman Chiang to preside over commission affairs are not true. Zhang's attitude remains passive and he will go to Wuhan to meet with Chiang, but the travel date has not yet been determined. As for the situation in Nanjing, the authorities are focused on rectifying internal affairs and construction in order to restore the old image. Yan Xishan has expressed that he will listen to the central government's arrangements for both domestic and foreign affairs. I went to Wuhan on the 9th of this month to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the situation in North China and stayed for two days. Later, Chairman Chiang, because Premier Wang was in Shanghai for medical treatment, ordered me to come to Shanghai to express condolences and urge him to return to Nanjing as soon as possible to preside over central affairs. Therefore, after arriving in Shanghai, I plan to meet with Premier Wang. Later, Mr. Zhang also stated to reporters that the sale of antiques by the Peiping Old Palace Museum is a matter that the outside world does not understand and has involved me. In fact, before Mr. Li Shizeng went to Europe, Mr. Li once consulted me about the position of director. At that time, I immediately declined because I was neither a scholar nor an archaeologist and not proficient in this matter. Unexpectedly, not long after, it was formally seen in an order. I immediately resigned, and although the central government did not approve, I still resigned forcefully.

Lin and Song Visit Wang: Mr. Wang was still not at his residence yesterday. At 2:05 PM, Song Ziwen went to Wang's residence to visit him, and was received by Mr. Wang's wife, Ms. Chen Bijun. As Song was about to leave, Chairman Lin Sen arrived, so they re-entered Wang's residence together and sat down for a brief conversation before leaving. Tang Youren visited Wang at 4:00 PM and left shortly after. Yesterday, Mr. Wang's residence remained guarded, and only his family members were busy coming and going. Furthermore, Ms. Chen Bijun carried vases and miscellaneous items by car several times in the morning, leading to rumors that Mr. Wang was moving.

Wang's Condition: Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Central Political Council, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. When reporters met him at Wang's residence at 4:00 PM in the afternoon, they inquired about Mr. Wang's condition. According to him, Chairman Lin (Sen) and Minister Song (Ziwen) had just left and did not meet with Mr. Wang. They met with Mr. Wang's wife (Chen Bijun). Mr. Wang is indeed suffering from illness. The normal blood pressure for ordinary people is 120, but Wang's blood pressure has recently been at 216. According to the doctor's examination of Wang's urine, not only is there a lot of sugar, but it also contains toxins. Therefore, Mr. Wang looks good on the outside. According to the doctor, if his blood pressure rises further, he will definitely become dizzy. The central government intended to have him and his doctor go to Nanjing together for treatment, and all expenses for diagnosis and medication could be covered by the central government. However, the doctor ultimately declined because the necessary examinations, equipment, and instruments could not be moved in a short time. Therefore, the matter was dropped. When Minister Song came to visit, Mrs. Wang gave Song the medical report to review. Therefore, based on this, it will not be possible for Wang to return to Nanjing in the shortest possible time.

Chairman Lin's Remarks: Chairman Lin Sen did not go out yesterday morning. Ye Gongchuo, Dai Kuisheng, Wu Kaisheng, and others visited him in the morning. Lin went out at around 2:00 PM and returned to his residence at 6:00 PM. When reporters asked him about the outcome of his meeting with Wang, he said that Wang's blood pressure was indeed very high and he was afraid that he would not be able to return to Nanjing in a few days. However, I did not meet him when I went to Wang's residence today (i.e., yesterday). Zhang Yuejun also arrived in Shanghai today, but did not meet Wang in the afternoon. As for Japan's recognition of the puppet state, it violates the Nine-Power Treaty and undermines China's territorial and administrative integrity. This matter will of course be handled by the diplomatic authorities.

Lunar Eclipse Tonight

Mid-Autumn Festival Evening on the Abolished Calendar

Partial Eclipse Visible in China

The Foreign News Agency reports that, according to the North China Daily News' September astronomical report, there will be a significant partial lunar eclipse on September 15th, visible in part of China (must be after midnight). The initial eclipse will be visible in Europe, Africa, the eastern Atlantic, the Indian Ocean, and Asia. The total eclipse will be visible in northeastern North America, South America, the Atlantic, Europe, Africa, and the western Indian Ocean in Asia. The details of the eclipse and the times are recorded as follows: The moon enters the penumbra at 2:05:02 AM, the moon enters the umbra at 3:18:02 AM, the total eclipse is at 5:00:05 AM, the moon leaves the umbra at 6:42:08 AM, the moon leaves the penumbra at 7:55:07 AM. The magnitude of the eclipse is 0.982, and the moon's diameter is 1.000.

Jilin

Volunteer Army Commander Li Du Reports on the Battle Situation

The Beijing Wenri Daily forwards a telegram from General Li Du of the Jilin Volunteer Army, stating that the middle route of our army, Yang Yaojun's brigade, occupied Shuangchengpu on the 微日(wei ri)日, cutting off the Chinese Eastern Railway and threatening Harbin. The commander of the right route, Feng Zhanhai and Gong Changhai, are leading their troops to approach Jilin, causing tremors in the provincial capital and panic among the people. Most of the Han officials have fled. The commander of the left route, Wang Delin, is leading his troops westward along the Jidun Road from Dunhua, threatening Jichang and coordinating with Feng's troops. In addition, Ma Xianzhang is leading a mixed army of 3,000 to attack Yilan. The vanguard has already reached the Yanwu Settlement, five li south of the city. The battles in Jilin, Harbin, and Yilan are fierce and are all in a stalemate. It is expected that they can be taken soon. The officials of the puppet state are extremely shocked, and the Japanese are deploying troops to provide reinforcements, but they are unable to do so in time and feel extremely uneasy.

Commander-in-Chief of the 3rd Route of the Northeast Volunteer Army

Zhou Han Arrives in Shanghai

Negotiates Assistance with the Support Association

Mr. Zhou Haitao, Commander-in-Chief of the 3rd Route Cavalry of the Northeast Volunteer Army, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday to negotiate assistance with the local Volunteer Army Support Association. The China East News Agency reporter specially visited Mr. Zhou at his residence yesterday. According to him, immediately after the September 18th Incident last year, he united the local militia and soldiers in the field to form the 3rd Route Cavalry Volunteer Army in October with patriotic comrades. They had fought fiercely with the Japanese bandits several times. After its establishment, many people joined one after another, and almost every village had people with guns who joined to serve. The people's anger can be seen from this. Later, due to financial difficulties and a lack of bullets, he had no choice but to divide the entire army and scatter them in Yixian, Dalinghe, Beizhen, Zhoujiatun, Xingcheng, Suizhong, Zhaoyang Temple, Beipiao, Lingnan, Chaonan, and other places, led by Wang Gechen, Zheng Xihou, and others, to continue the attack. He then came south to find a way to obtain relief. Fortunately, he received the support of General Zhu Ziqiao, so he happily returned north and reconvened a meeting of various comrades to plan the recovery of the lost territory. Although he is dull, he is determined to save the country. The troops in the Northeast fought with the Japanese bandits more than ten times. On July 17th and 18th, between Beipiao, Chaoyang Temple, Nanling, and Yixian, they destroyed the railway and, together with the Beipiao Jehol defense battalion, engaged the Japanese bandits, killing hundreds of them. Our army suffered only nine casualties, including the wounded battalion commander Zhang Shouzhen. When he left the Northeast, at 5:00 PM on August 19th, the Japanese bandits attempted to advance into Beipiao. A battalion of infantry stationed in Nanling, Jehol, engaged them. Our volunteer army divided into left and right wings, and on that day and night, they repelled the enemy, killing nearly a hundred bandits and capturing dozens. Our army is now moving behind the enemy lines between Chaoyang Temple and Yixian, cutting off their retreat and destroying railway bridges. Our army lost four soldiers and injured seven. Because our army adopted a policy of dispersing and regrouping during the counterattacks, waiting for work while well-rested, and using guerrilla tactics effectively, although the Japanese bandits' equipment was sophisticated, the volunteer army was eager to kill the enemy. It is a pity that there was no adequate supply of food and equipment. Therefore, he came south again to seek assistance from all parties and planned to contact the National Salvation Army's General Commander Zhu Jiqing's troops in order to unify command and recover the lost territory. The Volunteer Army Support Association is currently meeting on this matter and will return north in three or four days.

League of Nations Covenant Support Association

Informs Consulates and Businesses of Various Countries in Shanghai

Friendly Nations Treated Fairly by Us

Introduce and Promote Their Goods

The League of Nations Covenant Support Association, initiated by more than 70 important trade associations in this city, has received letters and telegrams from various provinces and cities in recent days, expressing deep sympathy for the association's organization and requesting the articles of association. Commercial groups in this city are also enthusiastically applying to join. The association sent a letter to the consulates and business associations of various countries in Shanghai yesterday, stating the purpose of the organization and expressing its warm welcome to the promotion of goods from friendly countries that treat China fairly, and expressing its willingness to take this opportunity to do its best to assist in the introduction. The original letter is recorded as follows:

To Consulates and Businesses: The Shanghai Cotton Cloth Industry, Paper Industry, Coal Industry, Hardware Industry, Silk Industry, and other more than 70 important trade associations, in order to deal with the encroachment on Chinese land by ambitious countries, based on the spirit of economic blockade in Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant and the principle of free trade for merchants, have initiated the organization of the League of Nations Covenant Support Association to implement an economic blockade against Japan. This association warmly welcomes the promotion of goods from friendly countries that treat China fairly and is willing to take this opportunity to do its best to assist in the introduction. International Trade Association

Advocates Common Trademarks for the Same Industry

Has Applied to the Ministry of Industry for Specific Regulations

Prevents Inferior Goods and Counterfeiting, Making it Easy for Customers to Recognize

The Shanghai International Trade Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "We have investigated the Trademark Law, which is intended to protect the interests of products, using special marks as product logos to prevent others from counterfeiting and making it easy for customers to recognize. Recently, foreign goods have flooded the market, and in order to facilitate their sales, some have even taken advantage of patriotic psychology, fabricated Chinese factory names, and falsely claimed to be domestic Chinese products. This kind of unethical behavior cannot be prohibited by counterfeiting trademarks alone. The loss of our domestic goods sales is even greater than other foreign goods, so we should quickly devise sanctions to try to plug the leaks. The sixth meeting of the Board of Directors of our Association has resolved that, according to the provisions of the revised International Convention for the Protection of Industrial Property Rights of 1911, various countries have enacted laws and regulations, and that corporations established by trade associations and operators with close relationships, in order to enhance their common business interests, may apply to the government to register national trademarks for use on their products and enjoy legal protection. In order to prevent inferior goods from being counterfeited as domestic goods, we can only follow the example of various countries and suggest that each trade association formulate a common trademark and apply to the Trademark Bureau for registration. All products of the same type, in addition to using their own factory's own trademark, should also use a common trademark on the product to make it clear and easy to see, so as to prevent inferior goods from being counterfeited and to make it easy for customers to recognize. On the one hand, the Ministry of Industry should formulate a specific law on common trademarks for the same industry to provide protection. We have already applied to the Ministry of Industry to stop the law on common trademarks for the same industry, and we have also written to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce to persuade various trade associations to adopt it. We hereby inform you, hoping that you will vigorously promote and persuade various trade associations to investigate and handle it." It is heard that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has already sent a letter to the relevant industries for investigation and handling.

The Japanese Consul Has Apologized to the French Consul

The Guomin News Agency reports that the case of the Japanese plainclothes police arbitrarily arresting the Chinese Pan Xiaguang on Rue Lubin in the French Concession has attracted attention from all walks of life. The French authorities also believe that the Japanese should not cross the border to arrest people, and have made a special protest. The second protest was made yesterday morning by French Consul General Meilai to the Japanese Consul General in person, protesting that the Japanese police did not follow the rules by issuing arrest warrants first and requesting the French police to make the arrest, and asked the Japanese authorities to pay special attention to the possibility of such actions causing disputes.

Yu Hung-chun Discusses Preparing for Autonomy

Funding and Special Zone Measures Must Be Determined Before Full Implementation

Neighborhood and Community Organization Cannot Be Altered by Municipal Organization Law

Yesterday, reporters visited Mr. Yu Hung-chun, chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Autonomy Preparatory Committee, to inquire about the recent progress in preparing for municipal autonomy. He received them and gave the following statement: Mr. Yu stated that since the committee was ordered to prepare for municipal autonomy, two months have passed since its establishment. The initial decision was to establish district offices in each district before the 15th of last month to begin surveying citizens, dividing neighborhoods and communities, and then proceeding with the election of autonomy officials at all levels below the district head. Therefore, at the beginning of the committee's establishment, an outline of the survey and election process was announced, with strict and practical regulations for each stage. However, due to funding issues, the plan could not be implemented as scheduled, and the special circumstances of the city, including special zones, are a major obstacle to progress. Due to the limitations of the facts, some adjustments may have to be made to facilitate implementation. Currently, measures are being drafted for submission to the central government for approval and active implementation. Once the funding issue is fully resolved and there are measures for special zone autonomy, the entire preparation for municipal autonomy will not be difficult to initiate and actively promote, so as not to fail the expectations of the citizens and the mayor of this city. As for the organization of districts, neighborhoods, and communities, it is stipulated by the municipal organization law. The current preparations for autonomy in this city are based entirely on the municipal organization law. Under no circumstances can the central government's laws be changed. Yesterday, various newspapers in this city carried my statement that the autonomy preparation matters will be adjusted, and neighborhoods and communities will no longer be established, focusing solely on election matters. This is a misrepresentation. Perhaps the so-called adjustment only refers to the special zone aspect, which still needs to be submitted to the central government for approval before there is a solution. As for the forty autonomous districts in this city, they must be handled in accordance with the municipal organization law under all circumstances, and no changes are allowed.

War Zone Relief Association Approves Huge Sum

Totaling 250,000 Yuan

The Wusong, Jiangwan, and Zhabei districts of this city have suffered greatly from the impact of the war. The post-war reconstruction and recovery work requires urgent funds. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly petitioned the municipal government to request the War Zone Relief Association to allocate funds for the relief of the general poor and displaced people in the district, who are suffering extremely. Upon instruction from the municipal government, the Relief Association approved the allocation of 250,000 yuan to the bureau to handle post-war relief work. It is reported that the bureau will receive the funds soon. In addition to using part of the funds as repair costs for the buildings of various charitable organizations in the war zone, the remainder will be lent out for the repair of civilian houses and for the use of commoners in starting businesses. As for the Commoners' Loan Office run by the bureau, it suffered a loss of more than 20,000 yuan due to the war. Now, the municipal government has allocated another 100,000 yuan as a fund, so that the Commoners' Loan Offices that were suspended due to the impact of the war can be restored immediately.

Cai Chang of Guangzhou Daxin Company sent a letter to the Guangzhao Public Association saying, "Guangzhao Public Association, respectfully, at the end of last month, there was a heavy rain disaster in the Dongjiang area of Guangdong, which caused the villages and towns near the river basin to become a swamp. The 50,000 yuan allocated by the government to Guangdong a few days ago is still waiting for Mayor Lin to complete the investigation in the northwest Jiang area before he can consider the situation. There will be no surplus money to relieve the Dongjiang disaster area. Therefore, we very much hope that the gentlemen of the Public Association will find a way to allocate funds in Shanghai to relieve Guangdong, and the people of Guangdong will benefit from the deep kindness and generosity. Academia Sinica

Continuing to Investigate Rural Economy

Ministry of Railways Agrees to Subsidize 300 Yuan Per Month

The Institute of Social Sciences of the National Academia Sinica attaches great importance to the research on the economic conditions of rural areas in China. However, due to the reduction of funding this year, the original plan could not continue, which is a pity. Later, the Ministry of Railways believed that the agricultural production status and the lives of farmers were closely related to the transportation and income of passengers and goods on the railway. Foreign-funded railways, such as the China Eastern Railway and the South Manchuria Railway, set up economic investigation bureaus or investigation sections to study and report on the growth and decline of agricultural products in the provinces along the railway as a reference for the railway bureau's funding. Therefore, there was also a plan to conduct rural economic surveys. The Academia Sinica specially sent a letter to the Ministry of Railways, requesting cooperation with the Institute of Social Sciences and funding to ensure that the original plan would not be interrupted. After receiving the letter, the Ministry of Railways decided that the Academia Sinica's on-site investigation of the economic conditions of farmers was a great achievement. It decided to entrust the original rural economic survey work to the Institute for handling and allocate a subsidy of 300 yuan per month starting in August. Yesterday, the Academia Sinica received the Ministry of Railways' reply, and the original plan will continue to be implemented.

Bombing on Rue Robert

Pan Yitai Rice Shop Bombed

Shop Assistant Gong Jingen Injured

At about 6:20 yesterday morning, just as the Pan Yitai Rice Shop at No. 4656 Rue Robert, east of the Great Clock, was opening for business, a man dressed in blue cloth shirt and pants, resembling a worker, walked to the counter, held a letter in one hand, placed it on the counter, and shouted, "Get out of here!" With the other hand, he took out a sulfur bomb from his pocket and threw it hard on the ground. There was a loud bang, and thick smoke filled the air. The shop assistants were terrified and scattered in all directions. The man, seeing that his purpose had been achieved, took the opportunity to escape. One of the shop assistants, named Gong Jingen, a local, 26 years old, was injured in the leg by the explosion, and blood flowed like a stream. A hole was blasted in the floor, and the cabinet and floorboards were slightly damaged. For a while, the doorway was crowded with onlookers. The injured shop assistant was taken to Renji Hospital for treatment. The relevant police station sent detectives to investigate the details. It is said that the shop received a letter on the 8th of this month, signed "Steel Essence Hot Blood Destroy Traitor Group," stating that it was secretly trading with the Japanese and supplying rice, etc. The shop ignored it, so yesterday another letter came, throwing a bomb as a further warning.

Record of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Statistical Society

The Chinese Statistical Society held its second annual general meeting at 9:00 yesterday morning on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. More than 20 members attended, including Tang Qixian, Hou Houpei, Li Quanshi, Sheng Jun, Sun Chaohuan, Lu Zongwei, Liu Zhigan, Chen Huayin, Jin Guobao, Liu Dajun, Zhu Junyi, Wu Dajun, Li Huang Xiaozhen, Lin Wei, Sun Zheng, Yang Runyu, Zeng Zhaocheng, Cai Zhengya, Chen Zhongqi, Zheng Xian, Wu Yugan, Liu Tiesun, etc. Chairman Liu Dajun reported briefly that last year, various agencies in Nanjing felt the pain of the lack of coordination and unity in statistics, so they invited representatives from various agencies to hold a joint meeting to establish the society. Last year, the first annual meeting was held in Nanjing. Next, Jin Guobao reported on the preparations for this annual meeting. Then, Lin Wei reported on the accounting and secretarial affairs for the past year. The total income for the past year was more than 300 yuan, and the expenditure was more than 70 yuan, with a total savings of more than 30 yuan. The accounts were audited by Wu Dajun, Chen Huayin, and others. Next, discussions were held: (1) Revision of the society's constitution (resolution): The clause in Article 21 of the society's constitution regarding the number of attendees at the general meeting must be more than one-third before the meeting can be held was canceled. (2) Location of the society (resolution): To be decided by the new executive committee. (3) Date of the third annual meeting (resolution): Changed to the spring holiday period around Qingming Festival in the spring of each year. (4) Publication of annual or monthly publications (resolution): To be handled by the executive committee. (5) Establishment of the Chinese Social Science Research Committee (resolution): First, contact the Chinese Economic Society for joint management. If not possible, the society will handle it alone. (6) Term of office of the executive committee members (resolution): The term of office of the seven executive committee members is limited to one year, and their term of office ends at the end of each annual meeting. Next, a general vote was held to elect the executive committee members. The elected members were Liu Dajun, Lin Wei, Sheng Jun, Sun Zheng (re-elected), Jin Guobao, Zhu Zuhui, and Cai Zhengya. Next, there was a public banquet by the National Tariff Commission and the International Trade Bureau. During the banquet, Vice Chairman Sheng Jun delivered a welcome speech. Next, Yan Jiguang, a representative of the International Trade Bureau, delivered a welcome speech. Finally, academic representative Cai Zhengya gave a reply. The meeting adjourned, and they boarded a car prepared by the Bank of China to visit the Bank of China. At 4:00 in the afternoon, papers were read. Paper Committee Chairman Zhu Junyi reported the names and topics of the members who were responsible for the papers. Then, the papers were read: (1) President Liu Dajun read "Using Statistical Methods to Study China's Silk Industry." The materials were rich, and there were more than a dozen charts, which explained in detail and were very valuable. (2) Zhu Junyi, Director of the Translation Department of the Legislative Yuan, read "Geographical Distribution of Historical Figures in China" (This book has been published by Zhonghua Book Company). (3) Wu Dajun, Director of the Central Bureau of Statistics, read "Comparison of China's New Statistical System with Other Countries." After the reading, President Liu Dajun reported on today's agenda. At 8:00 in the evening, they visited the Shenbao Museum, and at 9:00, they visited the Xinwenbao Museum. The general meeting will continue today to read papers. Today's agenda is to read papers at 9:00 in the morning (on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA). At 12:10 in the afternoon, there will be a public banquet by the Research Committee of the Pacific International Society of Chinese Economic Society (Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA). At 2:00, they will visit the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau, and at 4:00, the Shanghai Municipal Government will hold a tea party (Fenglin Bridge Municipal Government). At 6:30, Shanghai members will host a banquet for guests from all walks of life and members from other places (Zhongshe). Tomorrow, at 9:00 in the morning, they will visit the Kang Yuan Canning Factory and then close the meeting.

Ministry of Railways Questions Anti-Opium Society's Telegram

Responsibility for Transportation is Unrelated to Public Responsibility

To the Shanghai Shenbao Museum: Recently, the Ministry sent a telegram to the Shanghai Anti-Opium Society, which read: "To Mr. Wang Jingqi, Chairman, Mr. Li Denghui, Vice Chairman, Mr. Ma Yinchu, Ms. Ding Shujing, and all executive committee members of the Anti-Opium Society at No. 4 Hong Kong Road, Shanghai, upon reading the Shenbao of September 3, regarding the contents of the telegram from your society to the Supervisory Yuan requesting to stop the public opium tax, there are words such as 'The Railway Bureau is responsible for transportation, which is also related to the transportation of opium and soil. Whether this is true is not dare to say, but there is no wind without a hole.' Your society's mission is important, and issuing this irresponsible telegram is appalling. Responsible transportation has been implemented in the Northeast Eight Roads since the seventh year of the Republic of China, with remarkable results. The Ministry of Communications promulgated the General Rules for Responsible Transportation before the tenth year of the Republic of China, which can be verified. The Jiaoji Railway has continued to implement responsible transportation since it was taken over in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, which is also a fact. Last year, the Beining Railway worked hard to implement responsible transportation in order to compete with the South Manchuria Railway for freight transportation, which is even more obvious to everyone. This summer, in order to save the decline of freight transportation on various railways, the Ministry formulated procedures for implementing responsible transportation on various railways and prepared for the implementation of railways across the country. The warehouses and vehicles on the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou Railways were relatively complete, and the two railways were set up one after another. Regardless of whether the Jiangsu Province Opium Public Sale is true, it is not related to responsible transportation. Moreover, when the preparations for responsible transportation were completed and about to be implemented, there was no rumor of opium public sale. Where did this baseless talk come from, which is a gratuitous slander? The Daily News once published a conversation with Huang Jiawei, the director-general of your society, which also confused responsible transportation with public opium sales. The Responsible Transportation Committee of the Ministry of Railways sent a telegram to inquire, and only yesterday did the secretariat of your society send a letter, which stated that when the Daily News reporter interviewed Huang, he asked about the relationship between responsible transportation and public opium sales. Huang replied that he had not received a report on this matter and did not know the truth. The reporter then left. Unexpectedly, the next day, the newspaper published it as the official talk of Director-General Huang. The reporter had a misunderstanding. The news published by the Daily News was not a manuscript issued by this society. Therefore, your society has admitted that this news is not accurate. Why did the telegram to the Supervisory Yuan pick up baseless rumors again, which is contradictory? It must be known that in recent years, due to wars and banditry, the people's livelihood is in dire straits. Merchants across the country are under heavy pressure, and they cannot transport and sell goods safely. They only hope for the implementation of responsible transportation to relieve their transportation pain. The Ministry also knows that after years of military destruction, various equipment on various railways has been completely destroyed. However, they are not afraid of hardships and overcome all difficulties to make responsible transportation implemented as scheduled. It is the intention of the railways to strive to create a clean and honest transportation method for merchants. Unexpectedly, your society still forcibly introduced the theory of opium public sale, which is tantamount to destroying the only livelihood of merchants across the country. I don't know what your society saw and did this. Knowing that it is not true, you must slander it. I believe that the gentlemen of your society will not do this. However, judging from your society's letter, the blame for the slip of the tongue cannot be dismissed. Your society is a more organized group in Shanghai. If there is anything you do not understand about the government's facilities, you can inquire at any time. You must not use vague words to try to destroy it. If you must attach a bad name to responsible transportation and destroy it, then this is not what a wise man can bear to do. Moreover, the Chinese railways have no grudges against your society. If you say that using groundless words to slander heavily is enough to satisfy the selfishness of one or two people, then your society will not lack discerning people. I believe that you are well aware of the laws and facts, and you will certainly not be fooled by them. You should request your society to publish a correction in the newspaper immediately to clarify the facts. I am eagerly waiting for the Ministry of Railways to print the above. I hope you will check and reveal it. Ministry of Railways, Yuan."

Rice Milling Industry

Opinions on Responsible Transportation

Petitioning Party and Government Agencies

The Rice Milling Industry Association presented a document to party and government agencies regarding the responsible transportation of railways, which stated: "Recently, the Ministry of Railways issued Order No. 623 to the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations to promulgate the 'General Rules for Responsible Transportation of Railway Freight Cars of the Republic of China' and scheduled to implement it on September 1. Although it is a measure to rectify the railway administration, the complexity of its regulations and procedures, the high transportation costs and miscellaneous fees, are a severe hardship for merchants and people, and it is an unprecedented harsh policy. Therefore, all industries feel the pain deeply and are too constrained. They have risen up to fight hard and appeal for exemption. The association is engaged in the people's food, regulating supply and demand, and transportation interests are more closely related. The opinions on the difficulty in implementing the aforementioned transportation rules have been detailed by the same industry, such as the bean and rice industry groups, and reported in the newspapers. I would like to attach them here for your consideration. I respectfully hope that you will adopt them and revise them in accordance with the law. Moreover, food is the sky for the people and cannot be lacking for a day. Although China is an agricultural country, it can barely make ends meet in years of good harvest. In recent years, natural disasters and man-made disasters have spread across the fields. Even in Shanghai, the population is larger than other cities, and unemployment is increasing day by day. The national economy has gone bankrupt, and the poor are unable to make ends meet for the day. Rice is the most important thing for the people's livelihood and cannot be compared with other goods. Now that the government is considering the people's livelihood and exempting donations and taxes, it suddenly increases transportation costs and miscellaneous fees, which is like fifty steps laughing at a hundred steps. Shanghai is not a rice-producing area, and the food supply usually relies on the interior. In the event of a poor harvest, the interior relies on Shanghai for input. In terms of transportation, railways account for the majority. Increasing harsh and miscellaneous taxes directly harms merchants and indirectly harms the people. How can the disaster victims after the calamity bear this? In his previous speeches on the issue of railway construction, Sun Yat-sen said, "If there is no railway, there is no defense for transportation, and industry and commerce are abolished. What kind of industry can be planned?" That is to say, railways can revitalize industry, but if there is no way to transport, industry and commerce will be abolished. He also said, "You must know that the revolution is not the end of the career, and everyone can enjoy happiness. Please see the compatriots who are unemployed, hungry, and cold everywhere. Can we bear to ignore them and only take care of our own happiness? How can we enjoy it for a long time? If we want to enjoy civilization and happiness, we must first ensure that everyone in the country has a permanent job, does not cry out for hunger, and does not cry out for cold, and then we can say it." It is not just a portrayal of today's people's livelihood. He also said, "Only economic problems, when they are urgent, can only abandon the root and seek the tip, because the root is often lacking in immediate effect, and the tip can respond urgently. This is also in a helpless situation, but if the root and tip are not carried out together, there will never be a day of leisure, and it will continue to fall into the place of urgency." This is not just a针砭 for the improper measures of the Ministry of Railways today. The implementation of the aforementioned rules is like robbing cold rice from a beggar? Mr. Sun once said in the issue of railway construction, "But the sovereignty of the Republic of China lies in the people. If the people think it is OK, it is OK. If everyone thinks it is not OK, it is not OK." In short, Mr. Sun's words and deeds emphasize the people's livelihood and respect public opinion in every aspect. Benevolent words are beneficial to the authorities. How should they act in a practical way to complete the legacy? When it comes to railway construction, there are strategies and plans to follow, and the public has no objections. Now, the Ministry of Railways is abandoning the root and seeking the tip, reaching the President's painstaking efforts to save the people, and increasing the suffering of merchants. The association dares to express its feelings on the proposition of saving the country and saving the people, and express its feelings: "(1) Rice should be exempted from donations and taxes, and the transportation costs should be reduced. Remove the various surcharges, miscellaneous fees, and cumbersome procedures in Articles 10, 13, 14, 15, 25, and 29 of the rules. (2) Rice should be regarded as a special commodity and should have the right to prioritize responsible transportation, except for the restrictions in Articles 19 and 36 of the rules. (3) The unloading of rice should still be convenient for storing in the warehouse for six days as usual, and abolish the unreasonable extortion of charging fees for more than six office hours. The above three requests are completely petitioning for the people because they are not only about relieving business difficulties. I hope that you will respectfully submit it to the central government, order the Ministry of Railways to follow the rules, and take care of the difficulties of merchants and maintain the lives of the people. I cannot bear the urgency of waiting for orders!"

Two Railways

Employee Representatives Petition the Ministry of Railways

Requesting Relief Funds for Victims of the January 28th Incident

During the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, employees of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways disregarded danger and worked diligently, ensuring the safety of locomotives and passenger cars. They devoted themselves to military transportation and relief efforts, neglecting their families without hesitation. Once the armistice was reached, the entire railway network was restored within days. The patriotic fervor of these railway employees is truly commendable. However, the residences of employees at the Wusong Locomotive Factory, Shanghai Locomotive Factory, Shanghai Factory, and various departments of the General Bureau's Rolling Stock and Engineering Divisions were mostly within the war zone, resulting in immeasurable personal losses. Various parties have submitted petitions through the railway unions, railway administrations, and railway party branches to the Ministry of Railways, requesting the issuance of relief funds for the victims. The administrations have also forwarded requests to the Ministry of Railways, seeking the issuance of bonus payments equivalent to two months' salary, as per usual practice, to help compensate for the losses. However, despite the passage of many days, no effective solution has been found. Subsequently, employee representatives met with the bureau chief, but no satisfactory outcome was achieved. Therefore, yesterday (the 13th), on the night train, approximately twenty employee representatives from the railway's Rolling Stock, Locomotive, and Engineering divisions, led by Chen Bohua and others, standing directors of the two railways union, and Yin Maosheng and others, traveled to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Railways, hoping to achieve their desired goal.

Sanyou Factory Workers' Representatives

Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday

Demanding the Factory Issue Subsistence Allowances

According to Dagong News Agency, the Sanyou Industrial Company in Yinxiang Township has experienced a factory closure dispute. Following the municipal government's arbitration decision, the employer has expressed disagreement and filed an appeal with the court. Regarding the workers' subsistence allowance (840 yuan per period, two periods currently unpaid), the government had previously ordered the employer not to suspend payments until the dispute is resolved. Despite repeated attempts by representatives from the 7th District Cotton Textile Workers' Union, accompanied by party and government representatives, to collect the allowance from the company, the company has repeatedly refused, citing the absence of responsible personnel. As the rice shops could no longer extend credit and were urgently demanding payment, workers selected Xia Zhongzhao, Bao Boyi, and Gong Zishen as representatives to petition the municipal government yesterday afternoon. Secretary-General Yu received them. The representatives first described the employer's suspension of the subsistence allowance and the workers' hardships, requesting that the government order the employer to provide the allowance to ensure the people's livelihoods. The Secretary-General accepted their concerns and promised to instruct the Social Affairs Bureau to expedite the matter.

Qiuxin Factory Labor Dispute

Labor Side Asks for Contract Revision

Union Petitions Party and Government Agencies for Approval

According to Dagong News Agency, the Qiuxin Shipyard in the Shanghai Garrison has experienced a strike involving approximately five hundred workers due to the unjustified dismissal of workers. Mediation by party and government agencies has been unsuccessful. Currently, the labor side, respecting the advice of the party and government authorities and considering the floating dock project of the Bureau of Public Works, has expressed a willingness to compromise. However, the employer continues to insist on their position, making it unlikely that the situation will be easily resolved in the short term. Yesterday, the 1st District Shipbuilding Workers' Union, citing the Qiuxin Factory's failure to adhere to the labor-management contract since the appointment of a new manager, leading to frequent disputes, specifically proposed revising the labor-management agreement to fundamentally eliminate disputes. The revised agreement has been approved by the members' congress, submitted to the factory, and presented to the party and government agencies for approval. The original text is as follows: "Regarding the petition to revise the labor-management agreement, our union's labor-management agreement has been in effect since May 1, 1931, for over a year, and according to the agreement, it should be revised. Since the new manager, McDillory, took over factory operations this spring, the original labor-management agreement has not been strictly followed, such as the arbitrary deduction of workers' travel expenses for outside work and repeated unjustified dismissals of workers, resulting in repeated labor disputes. If it is not revised, more disputes will inevitably arise in the future. Attached is a copy of the revised labor-management agreement and a copy of the old labor-management agreement. We respectfully request your association (bureau) to review and record them, and we sincerely request you to convene mediation immediately to resolve disputes, which would be a great service. Respectfully submitted."

Anti-Civil War League Sends Letters to Honorary Committee Members

Informing Them of the League's Work

The National Anti-Civil War League, following its approval by the representatives' congress, has designated Xu Shichang, Duan Qirui, Xiong Bingkun, Zhu Ziqiao, Zhao Zhujun, Li Shizeng, Liang Yansun, Huang Yingbai, Zhang Zhongren, Hu Shih, Tang Weizhi, Wang Juantang, Yu Rizhang, Yu Qiaqing, Chen Lianbo, and fifteen others as honorary committee members. The League specially sent letters to each honorary committee member yesterday, stating: "Since the founding of the Republic of China twenty-one years ago, internal troubles have intensified, leading to foreign aggression. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Bankers Association, and the Shanghai Money Exchange Association, recognizing the necessity of internal stability and external defense, initiated the organization of the National Anti-Civil War League. After four months of preparation, 501 organizations and 1,057 individuals joined as initiators. On August 27th and 28th, the initiators' representatives' congress was held at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, where the charter was approved, standing committee members were elected, and the establishment of the National Anti-Civil War League was formally announced. In light of your eminent virtue and high reputation, leading the multitude, you have been designated as an honorary committee member of our League by the representatives' congress. With your profound concern for the country, you will surely satisfy the hopes of the people. Regarding the honorary committee members' work for the League, the League's second standing committee meeting resolved: (1) Honorary committee members may attend standing committee meetings; (2) Honorary committee members may provide guidance on the League's activities at any time; (3) Honorary committee members are requested to approve and support necessary work requested by the League. This letter is respectfully sent to inform you, hoping for your consideration. The nation and its people rely on it, wishing you good health."

Minutes of the Shanghai County County Administration Meeting

118th Meeting

The Shanghai County Government held its 118th county administration meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. The meeting was attended by the directors of the finance, construction, and education bureaus, the property director, and the head of the county government's secretarial section. The meeting was chaired by County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, with Hu Gongshou as the recorder. The resolutions of each case were as follows: (1) The County Magistrate submitted the Construction Bureau's proposed revised budget for the new road and bridge construction project, which had been submitted to the county for review. The meeting decided: (A) The revised budget will be submitted to the provincial government for record; (B) Bidding will begin on September 16th and will be opened on the 22nd. (2) The Property Department and the Education Bureau proposed that the existing land for the newly built residential houses is insufficient and that it is proposed to purchase farmland bounded by Zhuyehang to the south, Songhu Road to the north, Miaojing to the east, and the north-south road in front of the county government to the west, in order to develop. The meeting decided to purchase the land at a price of 100 yuan per mu, and the county government will issue a public notice to the Property Department and the Education Bureau, to be handled in conjunction with the 3rd District Office, and the purchase procedures will be completed by the end of September. (3) The County Magistrate submitted the Education Bureau's request to hold the second agricultural exhibition at the Farmers' Education Center. The meeting decided that the relevant tax authorities should collect products and actively prepare, and that the exhibition should be held at the new location in the spring.

Report from the Shaanxi Industrial Survey Team

Trip and Work Details

The Northwest Problems Research Association, organized by various circles and experts in the city, has been actively engaged in its work since its establishment. Members of the association, including Hu Shuhua, Guo Weiping, Gu Zhizhong, Zhu Qiqing, and Hu Juewen, participated in the Shaanxi Industrial Survey Team and traveled to various locations in the Northwest to conduct surveys, with the aim of contributing their findings to the central government and introducing them to the people of the country. Gu Zhizhong's "Western Travel Notes" have been published in the Shenbao and Xinbao newspapers in more than ten installments. Recently, Guo Weiping also sent a letter to the association's executives, reporting that they departed from Beijing on the 3rd of last month, arrived in Zhengzhou on the 9th, arrived in Luoyang on the 11th, and arrived in Xi'an on the afternoon of the 12th, and providing details of everything that happened along the way. Excerpts are provided below for your advance viewing:

The People of Xi'an: The people of Xi'an are honest and simple, retaining traditional values and living a simple life reminiscent of the agricultural era. However, due to years of drought, the people's 　 have not been enlightened, superstition is deeply ingrained, and science is difficult to accept. Furthermore, they are so preoccupied with survival that they have no time for hygiene. As a result, when epidemics strike, they spread throughout the province, leaving many bedridden, which is truly pitiful. Those villagers who manage to escape the disaster are mostly 　 due to their habit of chewing scallions and garlic. In Xi'an city, nine out of ten households hang a pair of red paper trousers upside down in front of their doors, and in the center 懇 there is not 　 . Some have tiger 　 and talismans attached, as they believe that this will protect them from epidemics.

Survey Categories: 　 The survey team departed on the morning of August 15th, and 　 immediately split into north and south 　 , with Chairman Yang Hucheng dispatching two companies of guards to 　 security and 　 garrisoning the troops along the 　 protect them. A discussion was held the day before departure to discuss everything, and Hu Shuhua was elected as the leader of the southern group, and Hu Yuanbo as the leader of the northern group, to provide leadership. The categories surveyed included: (1) Agriculture and Forestry (including forests, soils, climate, etc.); (2) Mining (especially focusing on steel, iron, coal, and petroleum); (3) Industry and Commerce (especially focusing on handicrafts); (4) Water Conservancy (including hydropower); (5) Transportation (roads and other transportation routes); (6) Economy (focusing on rural economy); (7) Special Products (such as medicinal materials and cotton); (8) Education (focusing on social education). The northern group consisted of eighteen members, along with accompanying personnel, totaling approximately thirty people. The southern group consisted of twenty-six members, including three agricultural and forestry experts, five mining experts, three industrial and commercial experts, two engineering experts, three economic experts, two education experts, and three journalists, along with accompanying personnel, totaling approximately forty people. As for the routes, both the northern and southern groups reversed their original routes due to the climate and the convenience of hiring mules and sedan chairs. In other words, they departed from the originally planned destination and returned from the originally planned departure point.

Team Members' Work: Among the survey team members, there were eighteen new and old members of the Northwest Problems Research Association. Therefore, in addition to collecting materials for the Longhai Railway, the team members also collected materials for the Northwest Problems Research Association, which were kept by member Yang Junmin for future exhibition in Shanghai to arouse the interest of the people of the country. Guo Weiping is currently responsible for investigating the industrial, commercial, educational, and economic conditions of Xi'an, while also presiding over the promotion of association affairs.

Association Affairs: The Shaanxi Industrial Survey Team, the Science Society, and the Shaanxi provincial authorities have joined the Northwest Problems Research Association in large numbers. Chairman Yang Hucheng, Pacification Commissioner Sun Weiruo, and Vice Minister Qian Zongze have all agreed to serve as supporting members of the association. Members in Shaanxi have proposed organizing a branch in Xi'an, which Guo Jun and the director of the Construction Department, Zhao Shouyu, the director of the Civil Affairs Department, Li Zhigang, the director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Li Xieji, and Hu Shuhua have convened, first holding a discussion to make proper arrangements, and then holding a branch establishment conference, which will be completed soon.

Land Reclamation: 　 Located 20 li from Xi'an city, on the south bank of the Wei River, there are 40,000 mu of reclaimed land, which is very fertile and suitable for planting cotton, rice, millet, and sorghum. However, it has been abandoned for many years and no one has paid attention to it. Now, many people are competing for the land. Member He Sui has claimed 500 mu, the Zhenwu Association has claimed 1,500 mu, and Mr. Zhang Puquan plans to claim more than 1,000 mu. The remaining land will either be planted by civilians or will remain barren. It is reported that the provincial government plans to use more than 12,000 mu of land to establish a large-scale farm. Guo Weiping and Hu Shuhua plan to claim 2,000 mu for the Northwest Problems Research Association for future use as a base for new villages or industrial experiments. Work is currently underway.

North-South Ocean Liners Stop Quarantine

The local port quarantine office announced yesterday that the quarantine of north-south ocean liners has been quite effective since its implementation. Recently, as the epidemic situation in Tianjin, Tanggu, Yantai, Guangzhou, and other ports has gradually subsided, it has been decided that, starting from the 16th of this month, sea liners arriving in Shanghai from Yantai, Tianjin, Tanggu, Guangdong, and other ports will be exempt from inspection, except for those with epidemic deaths among crew and passengers. Ships arriving in Shanghai from these ports will be allowed to enter Wusong without hanging quarantine flags. Each company is instructed to notify each sea liner to comply. However, ships arriving in Shanghai from Hong Kong, via Shantou and Xiamen, must still be inspected.

Reports of Gangsters Searching and Robbing on False Pretenses

Recently, on Edouard Road at the junction of the British and French concessions, from Dongxin Bridge to Zhengjia Muqiao, there have been gangsters impersonating detectives searching for contraband such as opium, taking the opportunity to seize belongings and escape. There are countless victims. These gangsters are numerous. If they find opium, they will force the victim into the Mantingfang and nearby alleys to extort money, even stripping clothes and shoes, stopping at nothing. Any resistance will be met with a beating. Yesterday evening, a villager named Xu from Gaoqiao Town, Pudong, was stopped and searched by the gangsters at the entrance of Baoyu Lane on Edouard Road. A box of opium and more than 30 yuan in paper money were seized. Because of the illegal possession of opium, he dared not report it to the police. Also, Mr. Cai Jishi, a lawyer, was on his way to the Second Special District Court around 9 am yesterday, on the Nanyang Bridge side, when three or four men in short clothes stopped the rickshaw, searched the bag he was carrying, and took out a gun to prevent him from making a noise. Fortunately, he was not carrying any cash, so he was only frightened and suffered no loss. Mr. Cai talked about it in the lawyers' lounge and felt that the world was full of thorns.

Boiler Explosion Tragedy

Yu Jinfat Burned to Death

At about 10:00 PM on the night of the 4th of this month, a boiler suddenly exploded at Maoxin Dyeing Factory, No. 24 Guling Road. At that time, Yu Jinfat, a Shaoxing native, 23 years old, and three others were on the scene, resulting in burns. Dai Jinshi, the manager of the store, found out and sent the four injured people to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, Yu suffered the most serious injuries and died at about 4:00 AM the day before yesterday. The hospital reported to the Xinzha patrol station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The body was carried into the Fielun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District District Court, was sent to the morgue to inspect the body. He questioned Dai Jinshi, a 34-year-old Shaoxing native who was the manager of Maoxin Dyeing Factory, who claimed that he did not know when the boiler exploded. The boiler was only bought three years ago, and at that time, it was bought in Zhabei and was warranted for five years. Now the store does not know where it is because Shanghai was at war. Yu Shuangbao, a relative of the deceased, also testified. Guo ruled that the deceased Yu Jinfat had indeed died from burns before his death and handed over the body to the elder brother of the deceased, Yu Shuangmao, who signed a statement to take the body back for burial.

Pedestrian Killed by Bus

At about 8 pm last night, at the intersection of Huade Road and Dalianwan Road, a public bus, number 15022, was driving from west to east at high speed. A pedestrian, Mr. Jia, about 30 years old, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers, looking like a worker, was unable to avoid it in time and was knocked down to the ground by the bus, injuring his head. The post patrol informed the fire department, which rushed to the scene and sent the victim to the nearby Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but he died soon after.
