The Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai held a regular meeting yesterday to discuss the amnesty of prisoners. The standing committee members Gu Zhuxuan, Cheng Xiechun, Jin Jiulin, Zhu Dexuan, Gu Songmao, Wang Kunyi, Zheng Jian, Zhang Ruiji, Liu Zhenqiu, and others, decided on the following measures: (1) Publicly appoint Zheng Jian and Liu Zhenqiu to take a letter to the Xinmin Fucheng Society to persuade prisoners to go to the West Prison. (2) Provide relief to the Jianghuai amnesty prisoners according to the list notified by the court, with the following measures: (A) If there are family members in Shanghai, the association will send personnel to send them back. (B) If there are no family members in Shanghai, the association will give them travel expenses to send them back to their original place. (C) If they are poor, they will be resettled after investigation. (D) Gather them in Shanghai once a month to encourage them to reform and not repeat their mistakes.

Yao Laixian Accused of Fraudulently Obtaining Property

Partnership to Open Dongxin Chang Customs Brokerage

Prolonging and Failing to Finalize Partnership Agreement

Yu Kangliang, a native of Ningbo, had been a partner in the De Yichang Customs Brokerage for many years. This spring, a Yao Laixian met Yu and, after a brief acquaintance, persuaded him to resign from De Yichang and start a new customs brokerage called Dongxin Chang as partners. Yao promised Yu a monthly salary of 120 yuan as manager. Yu was swayed by this and, in April, subscribed to three shares worth 900 taels of silver. He then resigned from De Yichang to take up his new position. However, after Dongxin Chang opened, Yao suddenly went back on his word, appointing himself manager and offering Yu a lower salary than agreed upon. Yu initially tolerated this, but when he repeatedly requested the partnership agreement, Yao made excuses, claiming that the capital had not been fully collected, and delayed finalizing it. Yu became suspicious, fearing that further delays would render his investment worthless. He then petitioned the First Special District Court for a provisional seizure of the customs brokerage. The court, recognizing that Yu had already paid 900 taels as security deposit, granted the request. The day before yesterday at 2 p.m., Secretary Zhu, accompanied by police officers, Yu Kangliang, and his lawyer Xu Fuji, went to Puai Fang in Maijia Circle on Wuma Road and sealed up the Dongxin Chang Customs Brokerage. Yao Laixian was out at the time. Employees and apprentices in the store moved their private belongings out. Yao was sought out and informed that the sealing could be avoided if he could provide the amount he was accused of owing to the court. Yao then went out to find a solution. By 6 p.m., he had raised 900 taels of bank notes and handed them over to Secretary Zhu, who took them to the court. The provisional seizure order was then rescinded. However, Yu still retained Lawyer Xu to file a private prosecution against Yao in the criminal court for fraudulently obtaining property.

Jia Songsheng Died of Anger After Being Extorted by Thugs

Jia Songsheng, a native of Xiashi, worked for a foreign firm in Shanghai. His wife, Mrs. Zha, and their eight-year-old daughter, Guilin, rented a house at No. 314 Pingji Li Road in the French Concession. On the evening of the 5th of this month at 7 p.m., Jia's daughter was playing outside with Fengxiang, the ten-year-old son of Huang Awu, a tea server at the Wanmao Inn at No. 401 on the same road. For some reason, they began to argue, and the two children got into a fight. After being separated, three or four thugs, protecting Huang's son, argued with Mrs. Zha about compensation. Yu Afang, the owner of the Yuchangxiang Paper Store at No. 309, intervened and had Mrs. Zha give the thugs 4.6 yuan as a "longevity gift." Because she had no money, her second landlord paid on her behalf. The next day, Mrs. Zha wrote to her husband, Jia Songsheng, to tell him what had happened. Unexpectedly, Jia, upon hearing this, fell to the ground in anger and died of asphyxiation. Mrs. Jia Zha, believing that her husband's death was caused by the extortion, filed a complaint with the French police on the 10th, accusing Yu Afang of bringing thugs to intimidate her. The police chief approved the complaint and sent Detective Wen Sheng to arrest Yu and send him to the Second Special Court. Yu was detained. Yesterday, Judge Li Changnian continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. The police lawyer, Gu Shouxi, presented the case, indicting Yu under Article 370 of the Criminal Code. The plaintiff recounted the incident. Yu Afang testified that he intervened to resolve the dispute and did not collude with thugs to demand compensation. He hired a lawyer to defend himself. The court ordered the end of the debate and scheduled the sentencing for a later date. The defendant was ordered to post bail, or be detained if unable to do so.

Six Robbers Sentenced to Imprisonment

On the night of June 9th, at 11 p.m., the Ruizhong Foreign Firm, owned by Liu Xianlie, a Ningbo native, located at No. 3 Tong'an Lane, Lao Yong'an Street in the French Concession, was suddenly invaded by armed robbers. The robbers confined the owner's servants in a room and stole cash, jewelry, and clothing worth more than 300 yuan before escaping. After the owner reported the crime to the police and requested an investigation, special agents from the French police successively arrested the robbers Li Ahong, Li Amao, Liu Guisheng, Jiang Desheng, Jin Rensheng, and Qian Jinshan, as well as suspects Zhu Yaxian, Zhou Xinyu, Wu Yingchang, and He Sifu, totaling ten people. A handgun and several bullets were seized and brought to the police station, then sent to the Second Special Court. A public prosecution was initiated for the crime of robbery by a group of three or more. After several court sessions presided over by Judge Li Changnian, the case was declared closed. Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., Judge Li presented the judgment in the First Criminal Court. Li Ahong and Ye Amao were each sentenced to seven years in prison. Liu Guisheng and Jiang Desheng were each sentenced to eight years in prison. Qian Jinshan and Jin Rensheng were each sentenced to three years and six months in prison. The number of days detained before the verdict was allowed to be deducted from the sentence. The handgun and bullets were confiscated. Zhu, Zhou, Wu, and He were found not guilty.

Husband and Son

Went to War Without a Word

A Woman Borrows Money to Survive and Attempts Suicide

According to Guomin She, yesterday a woman in her thirties attempted suicide near the Guanqiao Bund by jumping into the river from a ship dock when no one was paying attention. Fortunately, Zhu Haishan, the captain of the Shanghai Municipal Police Water Patrol, dispatched police to rescue her. She was saved and taken to the Relief Section of the Second Division of the Public Security Bureau for assistance. Xiao Shuying, a lady from the Relief Section, interrogated her. The woman refused to reveal her name. After Ms. Xiao repeatedly persuaded her, she finally said her surname was Wang. She had no one at home. Her husband and son had both gone to war several years ago and there had been no news from them ever since. As a result, she had borrowed money to survive, accumulating a debt of more than 500 yuan. Unable to repay it, she felt she had no choice but to resort to this desperate measure. She spoke through tears, requesting assistance. The woman had cut her hair and wore a diamond pin, a pointed face, a small mole in the middle of her right eyebrow, a wool qipao, a white striped Western-style short shirt and pants underneath, gray Western socks, and black satin shoes. It is reported that the bureau has sent the woman to the Xin Puyu Hall in the South City and posted a notice to find her family.

The Daily Progress of the Zhonghua Iron Factory

The Zhonghua Iron Factory, located in Lujiabang outside Xiaoximen, was established eight years ago and has been manufacturing machinery for various industries, receiving a warm welcome from society. Its various enamel machines are especially popular. Recently, the Qianghua Enamel Factory in Hong Kong commissioned the factory to manufacture a large batch of equipment, with the designs and structures being the latest planned by the factory. Special attention was paid to the selection of materials and supervision of the work. Most of the equipment has been completed and will soon be shipped. Given the efficiency of this equipment in enamel production, the entire batch was displayed in the factory. The factory specially invited people from all walks of life in Shanghai, as well as enamel experts, to visit the factory, evaluate the quality, and promote the products. Over twenty guests came to visit, including Zhang Gongquan, Du Chongyuan, Ye Youcai, Hu Xiyuan, Xiang Kangyuan, Zhang Huikang, Dong Xiyan, Tong Jitong, and Fang Jiangge. After careful research by the experts, all praised the beautiful design and excellent manufacturing, saying that it surpassed imported products. The factory then hosted a banquet. The guests and hosts parted happily at 3 p.m.

Datong Music Society

Second Batch of Domestic Dumbbells

Including a Pair Made of Ancient Wood from the Northern Song Dynasty, the Best

In addition to creating a complete collection of ancient and modern musical instruments, Datong Music Society on Songshan Road has also hand-made ten dumbbells, with materials, workmanship, and timbre comparable to imported products. Buyers rushed to purchase them, and they were sold out in less than a month. Due to social demand, a new batch of dumbbells in round and geometric shapes (40 in total) has been carefully manufactured, with the finest materials and methods. The weight is also light, making them easy to use. The bow is made of the most valuable wood, surpassing foreign goods. To promote the products, the selling price is uniformly low. There is also a special pair of dumbbells made of ancient wood from the Northern Song Dynasty. The timbre is exceptionally beautiful, long, bright, crisp, moist, and quiet. Eight characters are all present. The colored varnish makes them instantly recognizable as treasures. Unfortunately, only two were made, and they are intended to be kept in the society and not immediately sold.

Liu Ziyao Has an Affair with a Neighbor's Wife

Arms and Legs Slashed and Injured

Denies Having a Relationship

Liu Ziyao, a native of Wuxi and the principal of Renren Elementary School at No. 877 Yong'an Lane, Zhoujiazui Road, was resented by his neighbor Yang Changyuan, a native of Liuhe, for having an affair with his wife, Mrs. Shao. On August 14th at around 10 a.m., Yang Changyuan used a knife to stab Liu's arms, legs, and back more than ten times when Liu refused to lend him money. Liu fell to the ground and cried for help. Liu Baoshan, a Chinese detective from the Huishan Police Station, arrived after hearing the alarm and arrested Yang Changyuan. Yang Changyuan was sent to the First Special District Court and detained. The injured Liu was treated at Tongren Hospital. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong continued the trial in the Fourth Criminal Court. Police Lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that the victim, Liu Ziyao, had recovered slightly and was present in court. Liu, dressed in Western clothing and of imposing stature, claimed that he had established Renren Elementary School and taught English, while also working as a writer in a foreign firm. He had lived in the school for seven years and had known the defendant for four years, as he had asked the defendant to teach English on his behalf, and they had become friends. He had no relationship with the defendant's wife, Mrs. Shao. During the Dragon Boat Festival two years ago, the defendant moved elsewhere, then moved to Fuzhou Road. The defendant claimed to work in the Sino-American Clock and Watch Store and wanted to borrow 100 yuan, which he refused as it was too much. Later, the defendant moved back to Yong'an Lane and asked to borrow 50 yuan, which he still refused. On July 31st and August 1st, the defendant was seen pacing and acting suspiciously in front of his door. His wife notified him to be careful. Nothing happened for several days. On the 9th, the news article published in the Xinwenbao by a Mr. Jin, which damaged the school's reputation, was likely instigated by the defendant. On the morning of the 14th at around 10 a.m., the defendant was waiting at the entrance of the lane. Liu happened to be going out and met him. The defendant said, "I'm sorry for what I'm about to do to you today," and then stabbed him in the shoulder with a sharp knife. He urgently cried out to the shoemaker at the end of the lane for help, but was stabbed two or three times. He immediately fled, but was stabbed in the leg. He fell to the ground in extreme pain, then got up again and fell down again at the water tap, losing consciousness. He also retained Lawyer Shen Xingxia to file a private lawsuit. The defendant testified that the plaintiff's statement was untrue. He did teach English on his behalf, but his English was not very good, only knowing the ABCs. He broke off contact because of the plaintiff's improper conduct. He never borrowed money twice as claimed. He denied that he published the news article, claiming that what he published was against those who abolish the world's concubine system, not damaging his school. The plaintiff and his wife did have illicit relations. Because he was tall and powerful, he was very afraid of him. When the plaintiff came towards him with his head held high, he lowered his head and walked away. Their shoulders collided, and the plaintiff pressed him down and choked him, while shouting for the shoemaker to help him. He had no way to defend himself except with a knife. Cattle have horns, horses have hooves, and people have knives to resist. The defendant hesitated to provide further details. The defendant's wife, Mrs. Shao, was not very attractive, with a sallow complexion and unfashionable clothes. She claimed that she was first lured to a small inn near the Great World Theater under the pretext of watching a play, and then repeatedly had affairs with the plaintiff in her room. In court, it was said that Liu and Mrs. Shao were having an affair. Mrs. Shao said, "This is a dishonorable and shameless thing, you shouldn't humiliate yourself." Mrs. Shao insisted that she had been repeatedly raped by the plaintiff. Defendant's lawyer, Qiu Luqi, stated that the investigation found that the plaintiff and Mrs. Shao went to the Songhe Inn near the Great World on May 27th and booked a room on the third floor, using the names Gu Dehe and Gu Li Shi. The tea server saw that the clothes and appearance of the two did not match and thought it very strange, which could be investigated. Judge Shen ordered the defendant to be detained and rescheduled the hearing.

The Commercial Alliance of the Sixth Road of Zhabei

Responding to a Letter from the Commercial Alliance of the Tenth Road

Appealing on Behalf of Tenants in Shunji Lane

The Commercial Alliance of the Sixth Road of Zhabei, due to the fact that the landlord of Shunji Lane of the Yuyingtang (details reported in the ninth issue of this newspaper) was pressuring tenants, summoned a general meeting and worked together to assist, formally sending a letter to the Commercial Alliance of the Tenth Road in response. The public letter is recorded as follows. With due respect, we wish to inform you that the Yuyingtang Road in Zhabei Shunji Lane is heavily oppressing tenants, forcing them to pay arrears and ordering them to move out. The Zhabei people are publicly indignant. Pitying the common people in this time of disaster and unemployment, how can the government and the wealthy understand the difficulties of the people in order to revitalize the country? They are instead wantonly oppressing and arbitrarily destroying the people, not only ordering them to pay but even sealing and impounding their possessions, using every means possible. Their intention is to take the opportunity to increase rent and exploit the people. If this continues, further disputes will inevitably arise, and the Zhabei citizens will be completely forced to leave Zhabei. This method is not only an obstacle to the revitalization of Zhabei but also a blow to the livelihood of the people. For the sake of the livelihood of the people of Zhabei and for the sake of the revitalization of Zhabei, this alliance is deeply impressed by your alliance's fervent appeal and advocacy for the people. From now on, we will fight together, providing as much assistance as possible, striving to achieve the goal of alleviating the people's suffering, allowing the Zhabei people to have a way to survive.

Fourth District Public Security Bureau Cracks Theft Case

Recovers Thirteen Crates of Stolen Antimony Trisulfide

Zhang Peishan, a native of Zhenjiang, who resides at No. 150 Yunde Lane, Qingyun Road, operates the Huangshi Powder Factory. During the Battle of Zhabei, 125 crates of antimony trisulfide (used to make glass adhesive) were stolen. It was discovered that the stolen goods were hidden in a pancake store at No. 104 Wuzhen Road. He reported this to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau the previous night. Inspector Gong Zheng immediately led police to the address and found thirteen crates of antimony trisulfide (each crate weighing 100 jin), and arrested Ding Ronggen and Song He at the scene. After a brief interrogation, they were sent to the bureau for further investigation.

Shen Shouchang

Appeal Judgment on Child Molestation Case

Sentence Reduced to Seven Years

Shen Shouchang, a tailor from Nanjing, was sewing clothes in the room of Wang Boying, a servant of a Westerner, at No. 191 Jupeilai Road in the French Concession, on June 13th of this year. That afternoon at 2 p.m., Wang and his wife were out working. Shen saw Wang's eight-year-old daughter, Maomao, playing nearby. In a moment of animalistic impulse, he forcibly molested the girl. The mother and daughter discovered this and reported it to the police. Detective Wen Sheng arrested Shen on the 18th of the same month and sent him to the Second Special Court, which found Shen guilty and sentenced him to eight years in prison. Shen, dissatisfied with the judgment, filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Higher Court. The High Court accepted the appeal and held a hearing, declaring the debate closed. Yesterday afternoon at 3 p.m., Presiding Judge Lu Yimei, along with Judges Guo Dexin and Fan Peien, and the prosecutor, presided over the criminal court and ordered the appellant to be brought before the court. The court ruled to reduce Shen Shouchang's sentence to seven years. After the ruling, the appellant was remanded in custody to await further instructions.

Pan Lianshan

Will Die if He Cannot Marry the Woman

Pan Lianshan, the second son of Pan Yu'an, a native of Jiangbei, who lives in a shack by the railway in Tanziwan, Zhabei, is twenty years old. He used to farm in his hometown. Since childhood, he had been betrothed to Mei Yin, the daughter of Xia Deqing, a fellow villager. Mei Yin is twenty-one years old this year and lives with her father in Tanziwan. She works in a silk factory. Influenced by the prosperity of Shanghai, she thinks highly of herself and has long held the desire not to marry the rustic boy she was betrothed to in childhood. Pan Lianshan has now grown up and came to Shanghai from Jiangbei to request marriage. His father asked Xia about the marriage, but Xia and his daughter refused outright. After several unsuccessful requests, Pan Lianshan became so angry and anxious that he swallowed poison the night before last. No one knew at the time. After the poison took effect and resuscitation failed, he died shortly after. Pan Yu'an believed that his son's tragic death was caused by the coercion of Xia and his daughter. He filed a complaint with the Fourth District, and they were taken into custody for questioning. Yesterday, the district ordered the local security officer Zhang Fengqi to report to the local court and request an autopsy.

News from Trade Associations

The Materia Medica Trade Association held its third membership representative meeting the morning before last at 10 a.m. and re-elected the second session of executive and supervisory committee members. One hundred and five representatives attended the meeting. The presidium consisted of Fei Tinghua and four others. The meeting proceeded as usual. The chairman delivered the opening speech, followed by speeches from Zhang Dafu, the representative of the municipal party headquarters, Song Xiuqing, the representative of the municipal social, and Li Ruzhang, the representative of the municipal chamber of commerce. The chairman reported on the finances. Then, the representative of the Social Bureau drew lots, drawing out seven members of the first executive committee on the spot: Fu Huaizhang, Shao Quanfu, Yao Hongtao, Liu Zichang, Shi Rujun, Zhou Ruifang, and Xia Qizhen. The retained members of the executive committee were Fei Tinghua, Chen Wenming, Ye Chunqiao, Yang Liansheng, Yang Yangsheng, Kong Zhusan, Zhou Ziming, and Tong Zikun, totaling eight people. The elected members of the second executive committee were Dong Zhongxian, Hu Qibin, Gao Jianqing, Zhang Qinzhang, Mi Tingkang, Zhou Yushu, and Chen Yanling, totaling seven people. The elected supervisors were Xia Qizhen, Yao Hongtao, Shi Rujun, Shao Quanfu, and Fu Huaizhang, totaling five people. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding customs valuation, it was decided to have each trade association nominate a person to set a public price every three months. (2) Regarding resisting enemy goods, it was decided to continue efforts. (3) Regarding supporting the Alliance, it was decided to allow participation. Provisional motions: (1) Yi Cheng and others proposed that after the January 28th Incident, the Sichuan-Han gang switched to using northern rules for spot silver cases. It was decided that since the situation had calmed down, the original trade rules should be restored. (2) Guang Sheng and others proposed that the due dates for silver futures in other ports, originally set for March, June, September, and December, were now often chaotic. It was decided to publish a notice and set a deadline for settlement, otherwise, the matter would be dealt with by the last resort. The meeting adjourned at 4 p.m.

News from Various Trade Unions

The Shanghai Coal Industry Trade Union held its seventh board of supervisors and standing committee meeting yesterday. Zheng Xiaotang was publicly elected as chairman. The meeting proceeded as usual. The chairman reported on the recent state of the union affairs. Each committee member reported on the progress of their work. Discussions: 1. The internal affairs of the union need to be urgently rectified, as fee collectors are often engaged in embezzlement and fraud. What should be done? Resolution: (1) Fee collectors should report at 8 a.m. every morning. (2) Private collection for personal use is prohibited. Any violations will result in immediate dismissal. (3) Daily collections should be reported and reconciled on the same day. Knowingly violating this rule will result in a fine. 2. The union is suffering from a lack of funds. How should we find a way to make up the deficit? Resolution: (1) Fundraising is difficult, practical methods are needed. (2) Existing staff should fulfill their obligations. (3) Salaries will be started when membership fees can be collected, to meet expectations and comfort the loyal staff. (4) Collected membership fees must be publicly recorded, and no one, regardless of who they are, may seize them. 3. The union's registration is limited by funds, and the staff photos are not complete. These should be rectified immediately to facilitate the process. Resolution: (1) The photos of the directors and supervisors should be taken by the committee members within one week and should not be delayed, as this would cause inconvenience. 4. The last war broke out suddenly, and the staff dispersed. Comrade Yao Suikai, the director of documentation, also joined the army at that time. After the war subsided, the union, in order to resume union affairs, hired Li Zhineng as a voluntary secretary. It was resolved at the sixth standing committee meeting that a subsidy of ten yuan would be given for the month of June. Now that Comrade Yao has returned from the battlefield and someone is available to organize the union affairs, Comrade Li Zhineng is asked to seek other employment. Resolution: Passed.

Four Banks Issue Preparation Report

141st Report

The Four Banks Reserve, jointly established by the Yanye, JinCheng, Zhongnan and Dalu banks, is dedicated to issuing Zhongnan banknotes. According to the bank's articles of association, the banknotes issued are fully backed by reserves. Cash reserves must be at least 60%, and security reserves can be up to 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and the announcement is reviewed by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 141st announcement of the Shanghai Reserve as of September 10, 1932, is recorded as follows: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 18,800,7457 yuan. Total amount of reserves: 18,800,7457 yuan. This includes: Cash reserves: 11,611,876.87 yuan. Security reserves: 7,195,580.13 yuan.

Letter to the Editor

Dear Editor,

Regarding the Reuters dispatch from Peiping published in your newspaper on the 6th of this month, which reported that according to a telegram from Chinese sources in Xi'an, the Eurasia Aviation Corporation aircraft had two accidents in Gansu Province. The first aircraft, during a test flight from Lanzhou to Mazhou, crashed in Yongchang and was destroyed. The German pilot and one Chinese passenger were injured. The sixth aircraft, which flew between Lanzhou and the capital, crashed into a mountain. Two female passengers sustained minor injuries. It is now rumored that the Eurasia Aviation Corporation has decided to suspend passenger air services on that route, etc.

Our company's No. 16 aircraft, during trial flights to 州 and regular flights to Luoyang, did encounter accidents, but we have repeatedly received telegrams indicating that the injuries to personnel and aircraft were very minor. The Lanzhou airport was damaged by rain, making aircraft takeoffs and landings dangerous. Furthermore, due to the recent unfavorable weather conditions, we have temporarily suspended flights on the western section of Lanzhou. We are actively repairing the airport, and as soon as it is repaired, we will resume flights. There has been no decision to suspend services on that section. The Peiping dispatch from Reuters does not correspond to the facts. We would be grateful if you could promptly correct it.

Regular flights on the Peiping-West and Shanghai-West routes continue as usual. Suzhou, Hami, Dihua, Xinjiang, etc. are of utmost importance for international air transportation and the development of the Northwest. Although we have experienced minor setbacks, we will continue to move forward to achieve our goals as soon as possible.

Combined statement,

To the Shen Bao Newspaper Office,

Eurasia Aviation Corporation, September 13th.

Dear Editor,

I have just read a news item titled "Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association Meeting to Aid the National Salvation Army" in today's (12th) edition of your newspaper's local news, drafted by the Guomin News Agency. The content of the report is completely inconsistent with the facts. A Mr. Xie Jun came to the association the day before yesterday, claiming to have been sent by Zheng Guilin, commander of the 48th Route Army of the Northeast Masses' National Salvation Army, to come south to seek assistance. However, there was no official letter from the headquarters, and the route has someone in charge, making it unnecessary to provide direct assistance. The standing committee of directors has already made a decision on the matter. No plenary session of directors was scheduled for today to discuss assistance. The figures listed are also quite different from reality. The draft is based entirely on speculation and unauthorized proposals, which harm the affairs of the association. We are writing this special letter to request that you investigate and make corrections to set the record straight. We would be most grateful.

To the Editor of the Shen Bao Newspaper,

Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, September 12th.

Free Talk

Sayings of Ma Xiangbo, Nonagenarian

— Jing Ji

Problems Amidst Wind and Rain 丨 Agriculture, Industry, and Commerce

One Sunday noon, I was having lunch at home when a voice came amidst the wind and rain: "Mr. Xu, the old gentleman requests your presence!" So, braving the wind and rain, I went to the Leshan Hall.

It turned out that teachers and students from the Labor University Nursing School had come in the rain to seek assistance. The old gentleman instructed me to send letters to the governing authorities, the gist of which was: 丨丨

"The National Labor University has made a unique contribution to the promotion and improvement of culture in the agricultural and industrial laboring sectors in recent years, which the state and society should initiate and preserve. It is an unshirkable responsibility: Revival is easy... etc."

A few days later, I received a reply from President Wang of the Executive Yuan; the Labor University was given a lifeline. I also sent letters to Mr. Cai Yuanpei and others, urging them to revive the Labor University. The cautionary sentence personally amended by Old Man Xiang on the draft was: "Establishing a nation, culture comes first: Labor is the foundation of people's livelihood." Later, when I paid a personal visit to Mr. Cai at his behest, Mr. Cai indicated that he had received this letter. Old Man Xiang attached such importance to agriculture and industry, but he did not belittle commerce; and he advocated cooperation between agriculture, industry, and commerce, as the following matter can prove.

Another Sunday afternoon, with some raindrops adorning the scorching summer heat. I was commissioned to participate in the Central Business College graduation party; because it was an invitation from President Xu out of great kindness. Before leaving, I asked for instructions on how to word my speech. Old Man Xiang said: 丨丨

"Commerce must cooperate closely with agriculture and industry丨Otherwise, it is merely what is called peddling, earning a little money moving goods around," how could that be worthy of being called a merchant? Business studies must focus on the needs of the people's livelihood, such as how to tailor clothing materials from market cloth without wasting them. Merchants must plan together with factories. The sale of agricultural products is the same. I hope those who study commerce will broaden their horizons to study!"

Miscellaneous Notes of Fu Sheng

— Qian

(I) The Power of Officials

As the saying goes, "The poor don't fight the rich, and the rich don't contend with officials." In our society, even the richest people, no matter how powerful they may be, don't dare to contend with officials. The power of officials can be imagined.

I remember a few years ago, a person collecting house taxes came to my house. I said, "So-and-so's house is several times larger than mine, but the tax is not much different. It doesn't seem very fair." That person put away his book and said, "You say it's not fair? Come on, let's go to the county office together and argue." I said, "Okay! Let's go together." As a result, others pulled me aside.

I thought to myself, luckily I didn't go then. If I had gone, I would probably have had to sit in front of the iron window. Even though I am a follower of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the county magistrate would not necessarily talk to me about the Three Principles of the People.

(II) Dangerous Memories

Speaking of collecting house taxes, I was reminded of a dangerous incident. At that time, I was just a passionate and ignorant youth. After being scolded by the house tax collector, I couldn't help but feel resentful. So I wrote a large anonymous declaration, meaning that under the revolutionary government, the county magistrate was actually levying taxes arbitrarily and oppressing the people. We had to use the power of democracy to remove him from office. The declaration was written, but for some reason, it was not posted.

Looking back now, I am also glad that it was not posted 丨 If it had been posted, I am afraid that it would have been posted in the morning, and by the evening I would have been shackled and imprisoned. The next morning, I would have been escorted to the Guandi Temple outside the North Gate and executed by a bullet. The charge would have been "counter-revolutionary."

These things have all passed. Even that County Magistrate Yu is now nowhere to be found. However, I think that in such a large country as China, there are probably not a few County Magistrates Yu at present.

Witticisms

— Ti Gong

The red-turbaned Sikh watchman of the alley was arrested by the police for stealing from Mr. Zhang's residence and taken to court. Unexpectedly, Mrs. Zhang suddenly went to court and requested to bail the Sikh. The long-term consultant lawyer of Mr. Zhang's residence quickly called Mr. Zhang to ask what this meant. Mr. Zhang stammered for a long time and said, "This is probably my concubine's humanitarianism."

The owner of a department store invited Mr. Wang to dinner. Mr. Wang said, "Your company's great sacrifice these days has collapsed the copper railing. Isn't that deliberately taking a loss?" The owner smiled and said softly, "Among ourselves, it doesn't matter. We wouldn't really lose money. We'll just earn a little less." Mr. Wang went home, and his wife happily told him, "I cut six cheongsams at Company X today. The fabric only cost two dollars a foot. It was really cheap." Mr. Wang stroked his small mustache and said, "You are cheap, and she is cheap. It seems that the one who suffers is me."

The Lion Roars

— Fu Lei

Liu Shi's painting exhibition has already opened and closed. This is a gratifying thing. Because, in this time of war, chaos, and national crisis, the artist has not abandoned his cultural front and is working harder with extra caution.

Liu Shi is an extremely clever and quick-witted young man. I often advise him to be clever but not quick-witted in life, and to be an artist, he must especially have a bit of foolishness, which is of course far from quick-wittedness. Liu Shi is most easily influenced by others, because he is quick-witted. An unsuccessful work is of course inevitably influenced by others, but there is a difference between influence and imitation, and the result of quick-wittedness will often bury one's own personality and confuse influence with imitation. Liu Shi seems to have understood this point. His efforts over the past year have been to extricate himself from his hesitant, divergent, and depressed state, and to search for his own path with unwavering conviction. He is slowly abandoning likeness, ingenuity, and flamboyance, those superficial and dazzling techniques, and is experimenting with unity, purity, synthesis, and composure. In landscapes such as "Snow Trench," "Sound of Horns," "Eight Character Bridge," "Autumn Morning," and "Landscape No. 70," and in recent works from Putuo such as "South Heavenly Gate," there is this trend. The light and lively small techniques have disappeared in these works, and there is another kind of majestic brushwork. The bright and eye-catching colors he used to use have also transformed into deep, restrained, and melancholic melodies. Here, I am not saying that the use of color cannot be bright, but bright colors must not be vulgar, and must have a foundation. If bright brushstrokes can be refined from a deep and poignant poetic mood, then their brightness will no longer be superficial beauty but an expression of inner peace and happiness. The work "Sunset Glow" is a good example.

The three portraits of Miss Liang, Ms. Wen Zhen, and Miss Zhu are not only completely different from the twisted, fragmented faces of "Mother of a Friend" and "Miss Wenchen," but also attempt bold omissions, psychological peeks, and the modern interest in decorative style.

"Three Monk Stones" and "Portrait Sketch" (two works), and "Putuo Sea Bath" (two works) are the most outstanding and noteworthy works in Liu Shi's exhibition. "Three Monk Stones" is purely Eastern art produced by Western tools. This is a brand new and infinitely promising path. "Portrait Sketch" is rich in the charm of pastel painting, without the feeling of delicacy and astringency. It is a new discovery. "Putuo Sea Bath" is closest to the decorative interest of Dufy, but it cannot be compared with Dufy's innocence and detached mood. The boldness of the layout of "Snow Trench" is a significant success in Liu Shi's technique.

The current dark and chaotic era and country are the best opportunities to cultivate artists. Lion, you must remember this and not let it down!

Silver Threads (13)

— Jiang Hongjiao

(Seven)

"Is the madwoman upstairs surnamed Yuan?" Regiment Commander Yuan was in doubt, or perhaps motivated by curiosity, so he pointed upstairs and asked Fenruo.

"Yes, she's just a poor seamstress; it's a pity she doesn't have any family: the two of us rely on each other for life." Fenruo sighed and went to make tea, without speaking to Regiment Commander Yuan face to face.

"Since she shares my surname and is your good friend, allow me to go and visit her."

"No… don't go upstairs, she can't see strangers, please forgive me! Have a cup of cold tea and you should go to the meeting place." Fenruo handed Regiment Commander Yuan a cup of tea.

"Why don't you send her to a mental asylum?"

"Those with money are treated better in mental asylums; the poor who go in are simply entering prison. Apart from suffering indefinite imprisonment and dying inside, she will never see the light of day. Fortunately, there are times when her mind is clear, and she is just like an ordinary healthy person; when she is sick, I take care of her. We are all suffering people, helping each other is a good thing."

"How did she become mentally ill? Perhaps she suffered some stimulation?"

"I don't know the details. It seems she is a woman who was abandoned by her husband, because she has never talked about it; when I ask her, she doesn't want to say."

"This person is too pitiful; but are you willing to spend your whole life with a madwoman? Time passes so quickly, and there are so many changes in life. You should take care of yourself! It is best if you move to the city to live, and if you don't want to leave the madwoman, then move together, I should do my best to help you. Once you are in the city, you can also hire a good doctor to diagnose and treat her."

"We still want to solve our own lives. We have been used to living a hard life for the past few years. Going to the city would be inconvenient. But, I really want to hear you talk about your happy history since we separated. Please tell me simply, five minutes is enough."

"Fen! I'll just tell you one simple sentence, and you can imagine my situation in the past few years."

"What exactly is it? You must have added several children, as handsome and lovable as you."

"Alas, my Fen! I am still a widower to this day, where would I get children?"

"Then where is your wife?"

"Ever since I left 丨 Escaped from my home, my hometown, and joined the army, I have never communicated with anyone from my hometown. I don't know where my wife is. The young widow may have married a very good husband, and I hope that is what she did, as I expected; otherwise she must have died."

Swap Near… Amount Dried Up

New York Stock Market Plummets

According to a report from the New Harmony Foreign Firm, the New York stock market suffered a major blow on Monday (the 12th), a phenomenon unprecedented in the market in the past month. The market already showed weakness at the opening, and selling pressure increased, leading to a disparity between supply and demand, and prices plummeted. Although there was a slight recovery later, the results showed that each stock still fell by 3 to 4 yuan compared to the previous day. At the same time, because various railway stocks announced plans to reissue debt to repay debts due in mid-October, bonds also plummeted. Trading throughout the day was quite active, with a total trading volume of 4 million shares. Saying

The Awkward Literati

— Cang Ping

Cannot lift with their shoulders, cannot carry with their hands, and cannot make a living by selling and buying! This is the general reason for the awkwardness of literati.

Since ancient times, while some literati have been majestic and prominent, others have been destitute their whole lives. Flipping through ancient and modern novels, how many literati have truly distinguished themselves? And how many literati have died in obscurity, perishing their whole lives? I can say with certainty: of a thousand literati, one who can distinguish themselves is already an overestimate.

Alas! Literati have such a poor path, yet students today all admire literati. With great difficulty, they spend ten years by the window, only to find that in this vast world, there is not a single place where they can earn a meal. They retire at home, sighing to the roof, and only then do they lament! Unable to lift with their shoulders, unable to carry with their hands, they are not as good as a small vendor, who has strength and eats what they earn, and is free and unrestrained.

To be a literati of influence, of course, means "a pen sweeps through thousands of troops" and "a word is worth a thousand gold," but for destitute literati, no matter how brilliant your writing is, it cannot feed you when you are hungry or clothe you when you are cold. At best, you can file a lawsuit for someone, set up a fortune-telling stall, or write letters for others.

I am also a literati, because I have already tasted the flavors of a literati, so I shamelessly write this article (Awkward Literati) to inform future literati? I hope they will no longer bury themselves in dead books, no longer be refined and gentle literati, but quickly turn back, seek some practical skills, and compete for survival in this fiercely competitive world, and no longer be lifeless literati.

Art and Literature

Passing North Sichuan Road

— Ze Li

Horse tracks and the sound of cars stir up dust on my face, the flowers on the roadside are from the old spring. Tall buildings and mansions remain, with the slanting sun shining on people.

The mountains and rivers of the homeland have endured thousands of劫, the beacon fires and wars have turned to dust. Prosperity is ultimately fought for by people, but this place still presents a hundred shows.

Smoke and dust still resemble the colors of a battlefield, I revisit the old place after the calamity. Among the broken walls and ruins in the setting sun, it is difficult to ask passersby about the past.

Ke Ji

Talking About a Piece of Four-Dimensional Space

— Ding Chengwei

Originally, this four-dimensional space was a problem discussed in the theory of relativity. The principle of relativity is a very difficult thing to obtain, and it is by no means something that beginners in science can understand, but since I saw this problem, I felt that my interest in this problem was very strong. At the same time, I feel that there are many examples in our daily life that can be used to explain and illustrate four-dimensional space. Now I will give a few examples that are commonly seen in daily life and explain them with the simplest principles.

Before discussing this issue, we should first clarify the definition of space. In the past, this definition was simply that it could contain objects. However, since Einstein took the stage, he broadened the definition of space. He believes that space not only contains length, width, and height, but also time is an element of space.

In the past, Newton regarded space and time as two absolutely independent things, but after Einstein's theory of relativity was published, he included time in space and connected it with height to form four-dimensional space.

Page 21

What is the fourth dimension? Simply put, it's time.

Everything in one-dimensional space has only position and length, such as points and lines in geometry. They can exist in one-dimensional space.

Everything in two-dimensional space has length and width, but no height.

Everything in three-dimensional space has length, width, and height, with both position and volume.

Everything in four-dimensional space contains time in addition to length, width, and height.

If we use the coordinate method to express it, one-dimensional space has only one straight line as the axis (X-axis), but its two ends can be extended indefinitely. Two-dimensional space can be expressed by two straight lines (that is, the X and Y axes) perpendicular to each other on a plane. Three-dimensional space is represented by three straight lines (Y and Z axes) perpendicular to each other in space. Then, of course, four-dimensional space should also be represented by four straight lines (X, Y, Z, and T axes) perpendicular to each other in space. But in fact, space cannot have four lines perpendicular to each other at the same time, so here we can only assume that in addition to the three straight lines perpendicular to each other in four-dimensional space, there is also a dotted line that can be perpendicular to these three lines.

At the same time, Einstein also gave an example that is easy to encounter in daily life to explain the reason why time should be included in space.

Suppose a person is going to attend a banquet, then you must first know his address, in other words, you must first know the location of his banquet, which county, which street, which door number, which floor, which number, and at the same time we must know what time it is held.

In this sentence, which county, which street, which door number only tell you the position in two-dimensional space, which floor tells you the position in the third dimension space, and which time tells you the position in the fourth dimension space (To be continued)

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Remarrying and Remarriage

— Yi Ping

This is the most unequal issue between men and women. When a man's wife dies, he can remarry, but when a woman's husband dies, she cannot. As for men having three wives and four concubines, that is explicitly prohibited by law as a crime. It should be understood that the union of men and women should not be based solely on the premise of having offspring. Young men and women at a certain stage have the need to choose a partner of the opposite sex, which is a natural physiological tendency. Nowadays, with the trend of Westernization, marriage is determined by the individuals themselves, resulting in a false sense of freedom and rampant promiscuity, which is certainly not a good phenomenon. However, in the past, young women were not allowed to step out of their boudoirs, and yet books are filled with stories of illicit affairs. This shows that crimes committed by men and women are driven by physiological factors. However, I am not advocating for crime.

What I advocate is a monogamous system. When a man's wife dies, there is no question about him remarrying, as it is the custom. When a woman's husband dies, she should also be allowed to remarry if she wishes. However, if the couple had an exceptionally loving relationship during their lifetime, those who voluntarily wish to remain chaste should be respected, just as men who voluntarily choose to remain widowers are. But if one acts out of temporary impulse and later secretly commits immoral acts, they should be able to declare their intention to remarry beforehand, which would also protect the reputation of the husband's family. Because physiological needs are not something to be ashamed of, secretly seeking them out is considered despicable.

Furthermore, for economic reasons, if a woman cannot support herself after her husband dies and chooses to remarry, this should not be condemned. Although there is a growing call for women to have careers, how many can truly be independent? Who says that a woman should starve to death after her husband dies?

In my opinion, remarrying and remarriage are both perfectly legitimate. There is no need to pretend to remain unmarried and commit immoral acts in secret. As the saying goes, "That which cannot be spoken of should not be done." Things that can be openly discussed should not be done in secret due to social customs.

This is a very important issue that has not yet been raised by members of the social reform discussion group in this publication. I am unlearned and unskilled, and I am merely providing a starting point for this significant issue. I hope that fellow members of the group will contribute articles for discussion, offering insights and ideas, so that I will not have failed the author's original intention.

Family

The Third Secret Plan

— Shi Ben

Old Master Kong had just taken a charming and beautiful concubine, preparing to enjoy the delights of the bedroom. However, he kept thinking about how he had often heard that when someone takes a concubine, they inevitably become overly fond of her, listening to her every word and following her every plan, fearing that she might be hurt by a breeze or startled by a raindrop, leading to discord in the family and disharmony among relatives. This fulfills the saying, "If you want a family to be unhappy, take a concubine." Now, he was determined to stick to his principles and not indulge her excessively, lest she develop a spoiled and disrespectful attitude. He should make his own decisions independently and firmly reject any slanderous words she might offer, so as to avoid repeating the mistakes that lead to "family unhappiness"!

A month after the concubine entered the household, she observed that her husband's attitude towards her—affection—lacked depth. He was unwilling to accept her whispered suggestions, and she saw no sign of him transferring control of household affairs to her. She thought that if her husband remained so clear-headed and unwilling to listen to women's advice, it would be difficult for her to achieve her desires. Even her little sisters would laugh at her, calling her an incompetent fool who couldn't control her husband!

So, she decided to use a small matter to test him, to see if he would accept her words at all. However, the result was that the speaker spoke earnestly, but the listener disregarded them, showing no sign of acceptance.

She secretly plotted, "He is so determined to stick to his own ideas, huh? Bah! I'm not afraid. I have a way to manipulate you, to make you kneel at my plump legs and recognize me as your chief strategist, obeying my every command!"

That day, she put her plan into action. Seeing him enter the room, she demanded that he immediately build a separate luxurious house and separate from his first wife. However, after hearing her words, he remained noncommittal, showing no sign of agreement. So, she began to weep bitterly, crying and making coercive demands. However, his heart was as hard as iron, and no matter how much she cried and wailed, he refused to grant her request. Seeing that her first plan had failed, she proceeded with her second clever scheme, saying to him, "If you don't agree to my demands, I'll die right here and now!" Saying this, she ran to the bed, grabbed a belt, and put it around her neck, pretending to hang herself. But when he saw this, he

Page 22

didn't even glance at her. Instead, he ran outside! She thought that his old ideas were truly firm, and this clever trick of intimidation was not working. In that case, she had to use her third secret weapon to achieve final victory. So, she quickly threw aside the belt and hurriedly chased after him, embracing him tightly. With a face full of smiles, she rubbed her rosy cheeks against his beard and said coquettishly, "Don't you want me anymore? I can't bear to die without you!" At the same time, her two snowy white and slender hands kept caressing his body, up and down. Ah, clever plan! With this move, he immediately said, "My darling! Okay, okay, don't say that! I can't bear to lose you either. We'll move tomorrow..." Sentimentality for love triumphs over heroic spirit. His firm will was softened by her mesmerizing tactics. The next day, they indeed moved out. From then on, he could not help but listen to her every word and follow her every plan, fulfilling the policy of "family unhappiness."

Sin

What Will Be the Outcome?

— Ang Ying

Yesterday, I ran into Mr. Yang, and the first thing I asked him was, "Is your new wife good? Are you satisfied?" My question immediately made Mr. Yang's haggard face look even gloomier. I thought something must be wrong! I heard him say melancholically:

"Don't mention it! The new wife… I hate that demon!"

"So, you don't like her…? You're not married, are you?"

This question made his face even paler, and he said, "We… we're already married!"

"What? You said you don't like her, so why did you marry her?"

"This…" He seemed to have something difficult to say, but finally continued, "Old friend! You know, as soon as I stepped into my home, I planned to propose dissolving the engagement to my family. But when I raised this issue, my father roared like thunder, my mother wept and sobbed, scolding me for not being successful in my studies and becoming more confused the more I studied. They even opposed me objecting to the daughter-in-law chosen by my parents! Moreover, this engagement was made when we were children, and both families have good reputations. The next day, her father also found out and came to my house, saying that if I wanted to dissolve the engagement, he would sue my father! My father gave me an ultimatum, saying that if I didn't marry the Li family's daughter, he would tell me to get lost and never receive any financial support from the family… These were all cold arrows piercing my heart. Fearing that leaving my family and school would leave me without food (you know, can a college student find a job?), I succumbed…"

I took a breath and said, "So, you want to spend your life with her?"

"No! After I graduate from university and have a stable job, I'll divorce her!"

"As long as you haven't had any physical relations with her!" I said quickly. Mr. Yang's face changed, showing a painful spasm, and he stammered, "It's already happened! Ah!" When I heard this, I felt like a bucket of cold water had been poured on me, and I said to him bluntly:

"Old Yang! This is wrong! You say you don't love her and hope to divorce her one day; yet, you have physical relations with her! How contradictory! Those feudalistic people can use this point to attack you! How will you face the consequences?"

His face was pale, "But who will believe that we sleep in the same bed…"

"This can be verified by a doctor!" I said.

"So, what should I do now?" The veins on his forehead were bulging.

"What should you do? Old Yang! Don't believe that you'll have a job after graduation. Many graduates are running into walls. This marriage is entirely due to your own weak will, complacency, illusion, impulsiveness… How will you face the consequences in the future?"

Mr. Yang stared blankly at the ground. "The consequences?" he said in a trembling voice.

Chatting and Talking

After Awakening: Random Notes

— Wen Bing

(I)

Wearing a luxurious Western suit, with your hair neatly combed and chest puffed out, visiting stores or meeting friends at some large organization, the attendants there will treat you with special courtesy, taking advantage of you. Wearing a tattered long gown, you can stroll slowly by the roadside, and the beggars won't reach out to you: "Sir, please give me a copper coin"—this is also taking advantage of you.

(II)

In the past, if you paid close attention, whenever a VIP fell ill, there would be a change in the political situation, which was consistently accurate. Ah, how many secret schemes and how many sins are involved in this!

(III)

A friend who recently returned from abroad said, "China is a country where you can urinate anywhere." Thinking about this carefully, it is truly heartbreaking!

(IV)

When you are sick in bed, you will realize the happiness of being healthy, so "health" is the only happiness in life.

(V)

The dismissal and arrest, or removal from office, of Chinese military personnel are merely momentary tricks. After a while, they make a comeback, like a tumbler toy.

Market News

The Establishment of the China Women's Hairdressing Profession Association: Ms. Li Yunxia and Ms. Min Zhen, with the aim of promoting women's hairdressing, have initiated the organization of the China Women's Hairdressing Profession Association. The association will raise funds and entrust the Shanghai Women's Hairdressing Training School to specifically recruit free students. After they graduate, they will be sent to work in the hairdressing salons established by the association. Meanwhile, students will be recruited and classes will be opened in turn, gradually expanding to various ports at home and abroad. The first class has already been entrusted to the Women's Hairdressing Training School on Ximen Road to publish advertisements for enrollment. Those who are interested can go there to register and enroll.

Notice Board

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court

Civil Ruling: Zhu Ruixiang versus the liquidation office of Zhengyi Bank over a loan dispute. Appeal case (Main Text): The petition to reject the appeal is dismissed. The period for supplementing the second instance trial fee of $115.50 is extended to September 22nd of this year. ▲ Wang Yongkang versus Wang Nie over a loan dispute. Appeal case (Main Text): The petition to reject the appeal is dismissed. The petitioner shall bear the petition fee. The petitioner is required to pay the second instance trial fee of $216.30 within seven months from the day after the delivery of this ruling. ▲ Shen Zhongqin versus Zhou Mengfei over a Yellow Goods appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the second instance litigation fee. ▲ Liu Xiaobo versus Lin Hesheng et al. over a pawned cabinet appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the second instance litigation fee.

Civil Judgment: Yang Yi and Yang Chen Jinru over a dispute regarding the payment of alimony appeal case (Main Text): The original judgment is changed. ▲ The appellee's claim, the incidental appeal, and the petition for provisional execution are all rejected. The appellee shall bear the litigation costs of the first and second instances. ▲ Lin Jingde versus Xu Jinfu over a dispute regarding shares appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the second instance litigation fee. ▲ Jingfeng Factory owner Shen Hanqing versus Xielong Silk Store et al. over a dispute regarding payment for goods appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the second instance litigation fee. ▲ China Merchants Bureau North Pier versus Ba Heng over a dispute regarding compensation appeal case (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the amount of compensation and the litigation costs is changed. The appellant shall compensate the appellee with silver 1,729.9 taels. The remaining part of the appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of both instances shall be borne by both parties in proportion.

Criminal Judgment: ▲ Xu Huiqing over Liu Hongxun's breach of trust case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. ▲ He Yongnian et al. over a case of intimidation (Main Text): The original judgment regarding He Yongli and Zhou Amin's completed intimidation crime and the portion of the sentence regarding offsetting the prison sentence with days of detention is revoked. He Yongli is sentenced to four years of imprisonment for each of the two crimes of jointly intending to defraud and sending a threatening letter causing damage to others. Combined with the original sentence for the crime of non-compliance with intimidation, the total imprisonment period to be served is nine years. Zhou Amin is sentenced to four years of imprisonment for jointly intending to defraud and sending a threatening letter causing damage to others. Combined with the original sentence for the crime of assisting Zhu's... , the total imprisonment period to be served is eight years. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be offset against the imprisonment period at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The remaining part of the appeal is dismissed.

The First Special District Court of Shanghai

Civil Judgment: ▲ Zhu Guoliang versus Yao Yongyan over a car price dispute (Main Text): The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff with one thousand yuan and interest at a rate of 5% per annum from July 8th of this year until the date of execution. The counterclaim defendant shall return the check. The plaintiff's petition for provisional execution and the counterclaim plaintiff's remaining counterclaims are rejected. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Yise Sheng versus Jiang Zhengliang et al. over a loan case (Main Text): Jiang Zhengliang shall repay the plaintiff's loan of two hundred yuan in installments, paying twenty yuan per month from September 1932 to June 1933. The remaining part of the claim is rejected. The plaintiff shall bear two-fifths of the litigation costs, and Jiang Zhengliang shall bear three-fifths. ▲ Yuhe Pig Firm versus Guangmao Ham Firm et al. over a guarantee debt fulfillment case (Main Text): The defendant Guangmao Ham Firm shall repay the plaintiff's payment for goods of 224 yuan, 1 jiao, and 4 fen on behalf of Guangyu Firm. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the plaintiff and Guangmao Ham Firm. ▲ Alice Estate Agent Pan Shidun versus Jinlong Carpet Company et al. over rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant Jinlong Carpet Company shall repay the plaintiff with silver 600 taels. The defendant Wang Wenxing shall repay the plaintiff with 166 yuan and 4 fen. The litigation costs shall be borne proportionally by the defendants. ▲ Yeguang Company Baker versus Xiesheng et al. over rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant Xiesheng shall repay the plaintiff with 140 yuan. The defendant Zhao Shun'an shall repay the plaintiff with 156 yuan. The defendant Ruichang shall repay the plaintiff with 169 yuan and 8 jiao. The defendant Min Deji shall repay the plaintiff with 78 yuan. The defendant Cao Zhuyou shall repay the plaintiff with 112 yuan. The defendant Fusheng Restaurant shall repay the plaintiff with 96 yuan. The defendant A Bao shall repay the plaintiff with 160 yuan. The litigation costs regarding the parts of the claims against the defendants shall be borne by the defendants proportionally. ▲ Hartung & Co. Shen Licheng versus Jiangxi Jingde Porcelain Company over rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff with silver 1,393 taels, 7 qian, and 5 fen. The plaintiff's petition for provisional execution is rejected. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Ping Zhiming versus Chen Shengji et al. over rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant Chen Shengji shall repay the plaintiff with 315 yuan.
