The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Qian Tongrentang versus Yuexin Printing Factory owner Xia Genpei over rent and eviction case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff with rent of 560 yuan and vacate the premises and return them to the plaintiff. Provisional execution is granted for the eviction part of this case. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Hao Nanxing versus Lai Xuanqing over a loan case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff with a loan of 75 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Shen Yongxiang versus Xia Taigen over a lease right recognition case (Main Text): The defendant's construction work on the fence of the rebuilt building located at No. 881 Jing'an Temple Road shall be temporarily suspended. ▲ Ping Zhiming Company versus Ji Jinsheng over rent and eviction case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff with rent of 182 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen and vacate the premises and return them to the plaintiff. Provisional execution is granted for the eviction part of this case. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Wang Qingtuan versus Jiang Shouzhen et al. over payment arrears case (Main Text): The defendants Jiang Shouzhen and Jiang Caiyitian shall repay the plaintiff with silver 400 taels and interest at a rate of 5% per month from August 17, 1931, until the date of execution. If this cannot be enforced, the defendants Zhou Ziyu and Wang Zhensheng shall jointly repay it. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants Jiang Shouzhen and Jiang Caiyitian. ▲ The Public Works Department versus Jiang Zifeng over donation arrears case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff municipal tax of silver 39 taels and 2 qian. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. ▲ Lu Xingsheng versus Zhu Huifeng et al. over payment arrears case (Main Text): The defendant Zhu Huifeng shall repay the plaintiff with 700 yuan, with 60 yuan to be repaid monthly until the debt is cleared. If 200 yuan cannot be repaid, the defendant Wang Yu shall repay it on their behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Zhu Huifeng.▲ Li Xing versus Zhang A Gen's Tea (Main Text): The defendant Zhang A Liang, shall pay a defendant with 160 yuan. If not paid then the defendant Li Taodai shall reimburse; the fee borne Zhang A Gen.

Civil Instructions: Lin Yinfang's request for assistance in detaining Cai Ziliang for debt is approved upon review of the petition. ▲ Dali Foreign Firm versus Minsheng Paper Mill Zhao Guanqing over a payment for goods case. The request for execution is approved upon review of the petition. The case will be heard and a deadline for payment will be set. ▲ Bao Jiashan versus Xu Zhangyuan et al. over a rent arrears case. The request for execution is approved upon review of the petition. The guarantor shall be summoned for questioning. ▲ Ruichangxiang Firm versus Li Wangshi over a rent arrears case. The request for execution is approved upon review of the petition. The case will be executed upon review of the petition. ▲ Qiu Xinggen versus Zhang Zhaochun over a rent arrears case. The request for execution is approved upon review of the petition. The bailiff is instructed to evict the tenant. ▲ Shen Ziqin et al. argue against Zhou Futian. The request for relief is reviewed. The petition for relief by the petitioner has already been rejected by the court in a previous ruling. If they are not satisfied, they can file an appeal within the appeal period. The request is dismissed. ▲ Fang Wende and Evgeniia Bumbina's divorce. The divorce agreement and the request for registration are reviewed and approved for registration.

Criminal Instructions: Zhu Yunting's request to claim her son, A Bao, is approved. The Xinzha Police Station is instructed to hand over Zhu A Bao to the petitioner for proper care after he recovers from his injuries.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court

Civil Judgments

▲史金福 (Shi Jinfu) vs. 楊德聚 (Yang Deju) Eviction Case (Ruling): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲翁傳信 (Weng Chuanxin) vs. 楊良榮 (Yang Liangrong) Debt Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff the owed amount of 292 yuan in foreign currency. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲達理 (Darli) Agent 趙克恕 (Zhao Keshu) vs. 陳孚亮 (Chen Fuliang) Rent Arrears Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff 204 yuan in rent. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲張志銳 (Zhang Zhirui) vs. 張楊氏 (Zhang Yangshi) et al. Shares Case (Ruling): 張理卿 (Zhang Liqing) should repay the plaintiff silver 20,000 taels, with a monthly interest of 1% from February 23, 1926, until the end of the execution. 張楊氏 (Zhang Yangshi) may not manage the shares of the 申新紡織公司 (Shen Xin Textile Company) that the plaintiff is entitled to. The litigation costs are to be borne by 張理卿 (Zhang Liqing) by nine-tenths and by 張楊氏 (Zhang Yangshi) by one-tenth.

▲張長福 (Zhang Changfu) vs. 施托連洛夫 (Shi Tuolianluofu) Rent Payment Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff 135 yuan in rent. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲李盛衡 (Li Shenghang) vs. 李盛從 (Li Shengcong) Accounting Case (Ruling): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲泰利有期公司 (Taili Youqi Company) vs. 黃孝緝 (Huang Xiaoji) Rent Arrears Case (Ruling): The defendant should repay the plaintiff silver 612 taels. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲義和公司林錦章 (Yihe Company Lin Jinzhang) vs. 浦漲淇 (Pu Zhangqi) et al. Rent Arrears Case (Ruling): 浦漲淇 (Pu Zhangqi) should repay the plaintiff 120 yuan and 18 jiao in small foreign currency, 賀張氏 (He Zhangshi) should repay the plaintiff 90 yuan and 15 jiao in small foreign currency, 裕華廠 (Yuhua Factory) should repay the plaintiff 272 yuan and 8 jiao in small foreign currency, and 華新廠 (Huaxin Factory) should repay the plaintiff 200 yuan and 30 jiao in small foreign currency. The litigation costs are to be borne by 裕華廠 (Yuhua Factory) by three-sevenths, 華新廠 (Huaxin Factory) by two-sevenths, and 浦漲淇 (Pu Zhangqi) and 賀張氏 (He Zhangshi) each by one-seventh.

▲周生發 (Zhou Shengfa) vs. 顧新橋 (Gu Xinqiao) Land Base Case (Ruling): The land in dispute is confirmed to be owned by the plaintiff. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲陳奎福 (Chen Kuifu) et al. vs. 吳付君 (Wu Fujun) Deposit Case (Ruling): The defendant should repay the plaintiff 陳奎福 (Chen Kuifu) 3,600 yuan, with a monthly interest of 1% from January 1, 1931, until the end of the execution. The defendant should repay the plaintiff 浦康君 (Pu Kangjun) 2,150 yuan, and of the 1,000 taels of silver, 1,150 yuan should be calculated at a monthly interest rate of 1%, and the remainder should be calculated at an annual interest rate of 5%, separately from the date each debt was established until the end of the execution, along with interest. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲圓圓織造公司王禹功 (Yuanyuan Weaving Company Wang Yugong) vs. 盛鑫槎 (Sheng Xincha)俞禮坤 (Yu Likun) et al. Guarantee for Goods Payment Case (Ruling): The defendant 盛鑫槎 (Sheng Xincha) should repay the plaintiff 1,704 yuan, 1 jiao, and 5 fen, with an annual interest of 5% from January 18, 1932, until the date of settlement. If the enforcement of 盛鑫槎's (Sheng Xincha) property is ineffective, 俞禮坤 (Yu Likun) bears the responsibility for substitute compensation. The plaintiff's other claims are dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendants.

▲恊隆經租帳房倪雲來 (Xielong Jingzu Accounting Ni Yunlai) vs. 福泰豐主劉鴻冠 (Futaifeng Main Liu Hongguan) et al. Rent Arrears Case (Ruling): 劉鴻冠 (Liu Hongguan) should repay the plaintiff rent silver 784 taels and lane cleaning fee of 14 yuan, 于順興 (Yu Shunxing) should repay the plaintiff rent silver 200 taels and lane cleaning fee of 4 yuan, and 張政泰 (Zhang Zhengtai) should repay the plaintiff rent silver 300 taels and lane cleaning fee of 6 yuan. The plaintiff's other claims are dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by 劉鴻冠 (Liu Hongguan) by eight-seventeenths, 于順興 (Yu Shunxing) by two-seventeenths, 張政泰 (Zhang Zhengtai) by three-seventeenths, and the remainder by the plaintiff.

▲高永茂 (Gao Yongmao) vs. 郭榮記 (Guo Rongji) Loan Case (Ruling): The defendant should repay the plaintiff 1,500 yuan in foreign currency, with an annual interest of 2% from December 5, 2000, until the date of settlement. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲輔强車行葉善先 (Fuqiang Car Company Ye Shanxian) vs. 成大木行黃志賢 (Chengda Lumber Company Huang Zhixian) Settlement of Car Price Case (Ruling): The defendant should settle the car price of silver 180 taels to the plaintiff and pay the delayed interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the end of the execution. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲愛爾德公司 (Aierde Company) vs. 公道印書社龔湘舲 (Gongdao Printing House Gong Xiangling) Payment of Rent and Return of House Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff rent 148 yuan and 8 jiao and return the property at No. 1 Qingshun Lane, Rue de la Sainte Vierge to the plaintiff. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. This judgment regarding the return of the rented property may be provisionally enforced.

▲汪餘卿 (Wang Yuqing) vs. 汪炳忠順行 (Wang Bingzhong Shunxing) Bill Guarantee Debt Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay on behalf of 李開德 (Li Kaide) the bill amount of 600 yuan and pay delayed interest at an annual rate of 5% separately from the due date until the end of the execution. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲志平法律事務所江宗泮 (Zhiping Law Office Jiang Zongpan) vs. 周延祚 (Zhou Yanzuo) Payment of Rent Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff rent of 105 yuan and 7 jiao. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲余煒煊 (Yu Weixuan) vs. 榮李孝筠 (Rong Li Xiaojun) for Loan Case (Ruling): The defendant should repay on behalf of 榮文灝 (Rong Wenhao) 2,000 yuan to the plaintiff, with an interest of 5% per annum from the agreed repayment date until the end of the execution. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲長豐順沈沛霖 (Changfengshun Shen Peilin) vs. 答興逖百克房産經租處王大中 (Da Xing Di Baike Real Estate Management Office Wang Dazhong) Rent Reduction Case (Ruling): The plaintiff's request is dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲卓幹吾 (Zhuo Ganwu) vs. 江東恊記飯店 (Jiangdong Xieji Restaurant) Rent Arrears Case (Ruling): The defendant 江東恊記飯店 (Jiangdong Xieji Restaurant) should pay the plaintiff rent silver 2,320 taels. If the execution is ineffective, the defendant 葉淸和 (Ye Qinghe) should pay on its behalf. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendants accordingly.

Civil Instructions

▲沈翟氏 (Shen Dish) Requests Approval for Entrusted Execution: The petition is understood. A formal document should be prepared and sent to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court for assistance in execution, and the order should be delivered. The petitioner should immediately take the order to surrender and be detained accordingly. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 沈性正 (Shen Xingzheng) Petitions for Prompt Transfer of Case Funds: The petition is understood. Upon investigation, the case funds, totaling silver 1,138 taels, 4 qian, and 9 fen, plus 52 yuan and 8 jiao and 8 fen in foreign currency, were already transferred to the Shanghai Local Court by this court on August 29. The petitioner should directly apply to that court for approval to collect the funds. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 理 (Li) vs. 喬高斯基 (Qiao Gaosiji) Rent Arrears Case: Application for Execution: Upon investigation, in the case of the petitioner vs. 喬高斯基 (Qiao Gaosiji) for rent arrears and application for execution, this court opened a hearing on September 7 and instructed that the case be reviewed to determine whether the judgment was final before further action. Upon investigation, after the defendant 喬高斯基 (Qiao Gaosiji) appealed the first instance judgment of this court, the entire case file was sent to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for handling. It has not yet been returned, and it is impossible to determine whether it is final. The requested execution should be temporarily postponed. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 張漢 (Zhang Han) Applies to Revoke Provisional Attachment and Return of Security Deposit: The petition is understood. Permission is granted to revoke the provisional attachment and return the security deposit of 250 yuan. The petitioner should come to the court on the 17th of this month to collect the funds. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 泰愼洋行梅雪亭 (Taishen Foreign Firm Mei Xueting) Provides Guarantee and Applies for Provisional Attachment: The petition is understood. The petitioner should, in accordance with the ruling, pay a cash guarantee of 300 yuan before 12:00 noon on the 12th of this month for execution. The written guarantee of 300 yuan is clearly a misunderstanding and should be noted. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 唐惠卿 (Tang Huiqing)'s Agent 梅微閣 (Mei Weige) Applies for Release of Funds: The petition is understood. A letter should be sent to the Shanghai Local Court requesting the transfer of the case funds for distribution. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 林鴻泉 (Lin Hongquan) Applies for Continued Execution: The petition is understood. A summons should be issued for investigation and pursuit. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 楊福熙 (Yang Fuxi) et al. Apply for Registration of Leased Land: The petition is understood. Permission is granted for registration. The contract is attached to the file. This instruction.

▲一件 (One item) 顧金山 (Gu Jinshan) Applies for Continued Execution: The petition is understood. Upon investigation, this case was previously heard on July 21. In addition to the 20 yuan in foreign currency received in court on May 19, a balance of 140 yuan was still owed. However, on that day (i.e., July 21), the petitioner's agent, lawyer 宣震東 (Xuan Zhendong), stated in court that if the debtor 沈沛生 (Shen Peisheng) could pay the balance immediately, he would request a settlement for 130 yuan. The 60 yuan paid by the debtor in court that day has already been distributed. Subsequently, after adjourning that day, the debtor paid another 70 yuan to the court for safekeeping. According to the petition, the various amounts should be collected at the court at 10:00 AM on the 16th of this month to complete the case. Please take note of this instruction.

Shanghai Local Court

Criminal Judgments

Judgment in the case of 莊榮富 (Zhuang Rongfu) et al. for Harming the Family (Ruling): 吳阿鼎 (Wu Ading), in collusion, enticed 朱滿 (Zhu Man), a man under the age of twenty, away from parental authority, sentenced to imprisonment for one year. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. 莊榮富 (Zhuang Rongfu) and 秦根央 (Qin Genyang), in collusion, enticed a man under the age of twenty away from parental authority, sentenced to imprisonment for eight months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. 王鄭氏 (Wang Zhengshi) enticed a man under the age of twenty away from parental authority, two counts, each sentenced to imprisonment for six months, to be executed concurrently for a total of eight months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲Judgment in the case of 宋竇發 (Song Doufa) for Infringement of Freedom and Family (Ruling): 宋寳發 (Song Baofa) enticed a woman under the age of twenty away from parental authority, sentenced to imprisonment for five months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The public prosecution regarding 宋竇發's (Song Doufa) infringement of self-harm is not accepted.

▲Judgment in the case of 謝方榮 (Xie Fangrong) et al. for Harming the Family (Ruling): 謝方榮 (Xie Fangrong) assisted in enticing a woman under the age of twenty to hide, sentenced to imprisonment for six months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. 潘仁貴 (Pan Rengui) and 蔣洪生 (Jiang Hongsheng), in collusion, assisted in enticing a woman under the age of twenty to hide, each sentenced to imprisonment for three months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment, with a three-year suspended sentence.

▲Suspension of Trial of 謝錫榮 (Xie Xirong)

Judgment

▲陸桂林 (Lu Guilin) Fraud and Injury Case (Ruling): 陸桂林 (Lu Guilin) injured another person's body, sentenced to detention for twenty-five days. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day of detention.

▲Judgment in the case of 陳王氏 (Chen Wangshi) for Military Firearms (Ruling): 陳王氏 (Chen Wangshi) possessed military bullets without permission, sentenced to detention for twenty-five days. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day of detention.

▲Judgment in the case of 宋桂生 (Song Guisheng) for Embezzlement (Ruling): 宋桂生 (Song Guisheng) embezzled items belonging to his business, sentenced to detention for twenty days. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day of detention, and the two embezzled printing and binding machines will be returned to 馮夢雲 (Feng Mengyun).

▲Judgment in the case of 鍾順金 (Zhong Shunjin) for Counterfeit Currency (Ruling): 鍾順金 (Zhong Shunjin) received counterfeit banknotes knowing they were counterfeit and still used them, sentenced to a fine of twenty-five yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to the fine at a rate of one day for one yuan. One counterfeit banknote is confiscated.

▲Judgment in the case of 楊羣 (Yang Qun) et al. for Harming the Family (Ruling): 楊羣 (Yang Qun), 談滿堂 (Tan Mantang), and 趙老林 (Zhao Laolin), with the intent to profit, enticed women under the age of twenty, each sentenced to imprisonment for one year and six months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲Judgment in the case of 孫興餘 (Sun Xingyu) for Injury (Ruling): The public prosecution in this case is not accepted.

▲Judgment in the case of 丁樹泉 (Ding Shuquan) for Opium and Bribery (Ruling): 丁樹泉 (Ding Shuquan), with the intent to use for crime, possessed red pills, sentenced to a fine of thirty yuan. For delivering a bribe to a public official in violation of their duties, sentenced to imprisonment for two months, to be executed concurrently. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment, or converted to the fine at a rate of one day for one yuan. Four he of red pills are confiscated.

▲Order by the Prosecutor of This Court for Confiscation of Ownerless Smoking Paraphernalia (Ruling): Two opium pipes, three opium lamps, one opium smoking pipe, two opium boxes, and one opium scissor plate each are confiscated.

▲Judgment in the case of 周亭岩 (Zhou Tingyan) for Theft (Ruling): 周亭岩 (Zhou Tingyan) committed theft, sentenced to detention for thirty days. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day of detention.

▲Judgment in the case of 陳仲良 (Chen Zhongliang) for Opium (Ruling): 陳仲良 (Chen Zhongliang) smoked opium, sentenced to imprisonment for two months and a fine of fifteen yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment, or converted to the fine at a rate of one day for one yuan. Two opium pipes, one opium lamp, and a small amount of opium dross are confiscated.

▲Judgment in the case of 蘇子山 (Su Zishan) for Robbery (Ruling): 蘇子山 (Su Zishan) robbed another person's property, sentenced to imprisonment for six months. The number of days in custody before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

Civil Judgments

高海峯 (Gao Haifeng) vs. 周榮生 (Zhou Rongsheng) for Rent Arrears and Eviction Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff silver 90 yuan and 12 jiao. The plaintiff's other claims are dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne equally by both parties. Public Notice (Ruling): The judgment in the case of 朱拘生 (Zhu Jusheng) vs. 陳雲生 (Chen Yunsheng) for Loan Dispute is to be announced in the court's public display area (Ruling): The defendant should repay the plaintiff silver 1,000 yuan, with an annual interest of 1.5% from June 16, 1924, until the end of the execution. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. The above is to be noted by the defendant 陳雲生 (Chen Yunsheng). Judgment in the case of 蔡富英 (Cai Fuying) vs. 沈培新 (Shen Peixin) for Divorce Case (Ruling): The marriage between the plaintiff and the defendant is granted a divorce. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. The above is to be noted by the defendant 沈培新 (Shen Peixin). Judgment in the case of 王雨孫 (Wang Yusun) vs. 胡品三 (Hu Pinsan) for Mortgage Dispute Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff 300 yuan, with interest calculated at a monthly rate of 1% from July 16, 1927, until the end of the execution. If unable to fulfill, the mortgaged property should be auctioned off first to offset the debt. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. The above is to be noted by the defendant 胡品三 (Hu Pinsan). Judgment in the case of 凌濤 (Ling Tao) vs. 吳詠秋 (Wu Yongqiu) for House Appeal Case (Ruling): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant. Order in the case of 王進堦 (Wang Jinhui) vs. 蔣樹農 (Jiang Shulong) for Debt Appeal Case (Ruling): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant. Order in the case of 張鳳儀 (Zhang Fengyi) vs. 倪仰周 (Ni Yangzhou) for Goods Payment Appeal Case (Ruling): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant. Judgment in the case of 唐陳氏 (Tang Chenshi) et al. vs. 泰利公司 (Taili Company) for Adjacent Land Appeal Case (Ruling): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant. Judgment in the case of 杜宗高 (Du Zonggao) vs. 謝葆生 (Xie Baosheng) et al. for Rent Arrears and Eviction Dispute Case (Ruling): The defendant 謝葆生 (Xie Baosheng) should repay the plaintiff rent arrears of 700 yuan in foreign currency and vacate the premises. If 謝葆生 (Xie Baosheng) is unable to repay, the defendant 陳鳳標 (Chen Fengbiao) should pay on his behalf. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant 謝葆生 (Xie Baosheng). Judgment in the case of 王硯記 (Wang Yanji) vs. 殷長宏 (Yin Changhong) for Rent Arrears Dispute Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff rent arrears of 70 yuan in foreign currency. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. Judgment in the case of 王煥章 (Wang Huanzhang) vs. 方世根 (Fang Shigen) for Rent Arrears and Eviction Case (Ruling): The defendant should pay the plaintiff rent silver 252 yuan and vacate the one-story house located at No. 369, Tangjiawan. The plaintiff's other claims are dismissed. The litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff by one-twelfth and the defendant by eleven-twelfths.

Civil Instructions

一件 (One item) 鄭翊周 (Zheng Yizhou) and 徐金梅 (Xu Jinmei) Request Approval for Registration of Separation from Cohabitation Relationship: The petition is understood, and the attachments are noted. Approval for registration is granted. The attachments are stored in the file. This instruction.

一件 (One item) 鞠斌墅 (Ju Binsu) Requests Registration of the Seized Yongding Steamer and恳求(kěnqiú) Requests that the Navigation Administration Bureau be Consulted to Stop the Sale and Transfer of the Steamer: The petition is understood, and the attachments are noted. It is stated that there are many entanglements and the actual situation is difficult to determine immediately. The requested registration and consultation with the Navigation Administration Bureau should not be discussed. The attachments are returned. This instruction.

一件 (One item) 俞周氏 (Yu Zhoushi) et al. Request Registration of 俞奚氏 (Yu Xishi) Hiding Farmland: The petition is understood. As it concerns family disputes, approval for registration is not granted. This instruction.

一件 (One item) 朱懋功 (Zhu Maogong) Requests Registration of Acquired Shop Equipment: The petition and attachments are understood. Approval for registration is granted. The attachments are stored in the file. This instruction. September 13, Civil Judgment Judgment in the case of 趙林芳 (Zhao Linfang) vs. 張興記 (Zhang Xingji) for Loan Appeal Case (Ruling): The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant. Judgment in the case of 均泰莊 (Jun Taizhuang) et al. vs. 葉筱舫 (Ye Xiaofang) for Debt Dispute Case (Ruling): The defendant should repay 均泰莊 (Jun Taizhuang) standard silver 2,199 taels and 3 qian and 7 fen, and should repay 永豐莊 (Yongfengzhuang) standard silver 2,191 taels and 8 qian and 8 fen, both with an annual legal interest of 5% from May 31, 1932, until the end of the execution. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.
